TL;DR: 本文提出了 Every Eval Ever，这是一个旨在解决 AI 评估结果碎片化问题的标准化架构与众包社区平台，通过统一格式和开源数据库，极大地提升了评估数据的可访问性、对比性与科研协作效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前人工智能评估领域存在严重的碎片化问题，主要表现为结果格式不兼容、数据分散在不同平台，以及不同评估框架对同一指标定义不一致，这些问题导致研究人员难以进行有效的对比分析，阻碍了评估科学的发展、增加了成本并限制了资源共享。

Method: 1. 开发了一套统一的 JSON 架构，用于标准化元数据和实例级的评估结果；2. 构建了跨格式的自动转换工具，将分散在各种排行榜、框架和论文中的数据转化为统一格式；3. 在 Hugging Face 上建立了社区众包数据库，通过版本控制和协作方式聚合和管理全球的人工智能评估结果。

Result: 构建了涵盖 22,235 个模型、2,273 个独立基准测试和 31 种评估格式的全球性共享数据库。该项目实现了评估结果的标准化存储与互操作，极大地简化了跨平台的数据检索与分析流程。

Conclusion: 通过引入 Every Eval Ever，作者成功建立了一个标准化的评估结果共享生态。这一标准化框架不仅解决了数据孤岛和格式不兼容的问题，还通过社区驱动的模式极大地增强了人工智能评估的透明度、可复现性和科研效率，为评估科学的进一步发展奠定了基础。

Abstract: AI evaluations are widely used for testing and understanding progress. However, the diverse evaluators bring with them inconsistencies that challenge analysis and comparison. First, results are saved in incompatible formats, scattered across leaderboards, papers, blog posts, evaluation harness logs, and custom repositories. Second, results are created by different evaluation frameworks, which produce divergent scores for nominally identical evaluations and record metadata inconsistently, hindering comparison, cross-community evaluation science, cost reduction, and reuse. We introduce Every Eval Ever, the first shared schema and community-crowdsourced repository for AI evaluation results. The schema standardizes how evaluations are represented in a unified, single JSON document. It is source-agnostic by design, ingesting results from evaluation harnesses and papers alike, and optionally stores per-instance outputs for fine-grained analysis. We contribute: (i) a community-governed metadata schema with a companion instance-level schema, the first standardization effort of its kind; (ii) automatic converters from popular formats, evaluation harnesses, and leaderboards to the unified schema; and (iii) a crowdsourced community database hosted on Hugging Face, currently spanning to date 22,235 models, 2,273 unique benchmarks, and 31 evaluation formats.

### [80] [StreamMemBench: Streaming Evaluation of Agent Memory for Future-Oriented Assistance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14571)
*Guanming Liu,Yuqi Ren,Hansu Gu,Peng Zhang,Weihang Wang,Jiahao Liu,Ning Gu,Tun Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 StreamMemBench，这是一个用于评估个人智能体流式记忆能力的新基准。研究发现，尽管现有系统能存储部分数据，但在将日常观察和反馈转化为持续、有效的未来辅助行为方面仍存在明显短板。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的记忆基准测试通常将对话回忆或任务改进孤立地进行评估，缺乏对从流式观察到持续辅助这一完整路径的系统性测试。因此，研究旨在评估智能体是否能够真正地利用日常交互中的观察线索和反馈，并将其应用于未来的类似任务中。

Method: 该研究提出了一个名为 StreamMemBench 的流式基准测试。它基于 EgoLife 自我中心视角视频流，构建了以“证据锚点”为核心的两阶段任务序列：第一阶段测试对观察证据的使用能力，第二阶段测试对交互反馈和经验的重用能力。同时，研究定义了四项核心指标来分别诊断证据检索、初步使用、反馈整合及后续重用情况。

Result: 通过对八种不同记忆系统在两种骨干模型上的测试，结果表明：即使证据已被存储或反馈已被局部整合，现有系统在将观测到的证据转化为可靠的后续行为方面仍然表现较差，未能有效地实现长期记忆的迁移和重用。

Conclusion: 现有的大多数个人智能体记忆系统在处理流式观察数据时表现不佳，特别是在将历史观察证据转化为后续任务的辅助能力上存在显著缺口。该研究强调了开发能够真正实现长期记忆重用和持续交互学习系统的必要性。

Abstract: A central role of personal-agent memory is to turn stored information and prior interactions into future-oriented assistance. In daily use, useful cues come from what the agent observes and how the user interacts with the agent, and the agent must carry them forward from the current request to similar future tasks. Existing memory benchmarks usually test dialogue recall or task improvement in isolation, leaving the trajectory from streaming observations to later assistance largely untested. We introduce StreamMemBench, a streaming benchmark that constructs a two-step task sequence around each evidence anchor from EgoLife egocentric streams. The initial task tests evidence use, while the follow-up task tests whether feedback and interaction experience are reused. Four metrics diagnose evidence recall, initial evidence use, feedback incorporation, and follow-up reuse. Experiments with eight memory systems across two backbones show that current systems often fail to use observed evidence or turn feedback into reliable follow-up behavior, even when evidence is stored or feedback is incorporated locally. StreamMemBench is publicly available at https://github.com/landian60/StreamMemBench.

### [81] [VISTA: View-Consistent Self-Verified Training for GUI Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14579)
*Xinyu Qiu,Yunzhu Zhang,Heng Jia,Shuheng Shen,Changhua Meng,Linchao Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: VISTA框架通过构建多视图GUI采样组和引入自我验证锚点，优化了GRPO在GUI定位任务中的训练效率，显著提升了模型在不同复杂程度界面下的定位精度与稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在使用GRPO进行GUI Grounding时，由于从单一视图采样，模型容易在简单样本上全部成功或在困难样本上全部失败，导致缺乏有效的奖励对比，无法提供训练所需的相对优势信号。

Method: 1. 多视图构建：通过对同一GUI界面进行不同裁剪（保留目标元素及其坐标映射），生成语义等价但几何表现不同的视图，构建GRPO训练组。 2. 自我验证机制（Self-Verified Cross-View Anchor）：引入一个优势加权损失的“预言家”答案，作为锚点，仅在模型产生最大奖励时激活，旨在稳定坐标生成的训练，避免模型坍缩为无条件模仿。

Result: VISTA在五个GUI定位基准测试中表现出色，在ScreenSpot-Pro上，将Qwen3-VL各版本模型的准确率提升了约8%-14%，并显著降低了预测波动率，提升了最差视图下的准确率。

Conclusion: VISTA通过引入多视图一致性训练和自我验证机制，有效解决了GUI Grounding任务中GRPO方法在难度极端样本上难以提供有效相对优势的问题。该方法在多项基准测试中显著提升了模型的定位准确性与鲁棒性。

Abstract: When applying Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for GUI Grounding, rollouts are sampled from a single screenshot view; groups often become either all failures on difficult instances or all successes on easy ones, yielding no useful relative advantage. We propose VISTA (View-Consistent Self-Verified Training), a GRPO-based training framework that constructs each comparison group from multiple target-preserving views of the same GUI instance.Each view is generated by a crop that keeps the target element visible and remaps its box exactly, so model rollouts are compared across semantically equivalent but geometrically different inputs. To stabilize short coordinate generation without turning reinforcement learning into unconditional imitation, VISTA further adds a self-verified cross-view anchor: an oracle answer optimized with an advantage-weighted loss, excluded from the group baseline and activated only when the model has produced a maximum-reward rollout. Across five GUI-grounding benchmarks and multiple Qwen backbones, VISTA consistently improves grounding accuracy.On ScreenSpot-Pro, it raises Qwen3-VL 4B/8B/30B-A3B from 55.5/52.7/53.7 to 63.4/65.8/67.0. Robustness analyses further show higher worst-view accuracy and lower prediction flip rates.

</details>


### [82] [A Temporal Planning Framework for Disruption Aware Dynamic Route Optimization in Heterogeneous Railway Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14582)
*Pollob Chandra Ray,Sabah Binte Noor,Fazlul Hasan Siddiqui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于PDDL 2.1时态规划的铁路动态路径优化框架，通过自动化建模解决了异构铁路网络中的轨道切换、多轨距约束及突发中断管理问题，有效提升了运行的安全性和效率。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于时态规划（Temporal Planning）的框架，利用PDDL 2.1语言对铁路运行建模，明确定义了轨距兼容性约束及各类中断场景，通过时态规划器生成包含精确时间戳的无冲突运行计划和可执行动作序列。

Result: 在包含200个实例、最高达1000个轨道点和120列火车的基准测试中，该框架成功生成了有效的时态运行计划，能够处理多轨距约束及各种随机中断，验证了其在复杂场景下的适用性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于时态规划（PDDL 2.1）的方法能够有效解决异构铁路网络中的动态路径优化与中断管理问题，显著降低了对人工操作的依赖，提高了铁路运行的安全性和自动化水平。

Abstract: Efficient route optimization play a vital role in ensuring both safety and punctuality in railway operations. It is very crucial particularly in heterogeneous multi-gauge railway networks with varying train speed, stopping pattern, infrastructure compatibility constraints increase coordination complexity. In single-track systems these challenges are further intensify due to all trains to share the same track and requires frequent track switching.Stochastic disruptions events including blocked tracks, blocked trains, engine failure and speed slowdowns introduces additional unpredictability in operations and deviate the timetable. However, existing studies predominantly focuses on high-level timetabling, omitting operational details such as track switching coordination. As a result leaving decision to human operators, increasing safety risks into railway operations. This study proposes a framework based on temporal planning for dynamic route optimization and disruption management in heterogeneous railway systems. The framework formulates railway operations as a temporal planning problem using PDDL 2.1 with explicitly modeling gauge compatibility constraints and diverse disruption scenarios. It generates conflict-free timestamped operational plans specifying both optimized schedules and executable action sequences. To evaluate the proposed framework, we developed a benchmark problem set with 200 instances using up to 1,000 track points and 120 trains. Two state-of-the-art temporal planners and a plan validator were employed to assessed the framework. The experimental results demonstrate that the framework effectively generates temporal operational plans for heterogeneous railway systems and handles multi-gauge constraints, disruptions, and reduces dependence on manual decision making.

### [83] [Abstracting Cross-Domain Action Sequences into Interpretable Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14654)
*Gaurav Verma,Scott Counts*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究引入了WorkflowView框架，利用大语言模型将杂乱的低级用户交互日志抽象为具有语义的高级活动，在多个任务中表现出优异的泛化能力和准确性，为数字行为分析提供了一种高效的新方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字应用交互日志虽然记录了详尽的操作轨迹，但由于粒度过细且噪声较大，难以提取出对改进数字产品至关重要的用户工作流洞察。现有的基于深度学习的聚类方法对噪声高度敏感，且难以跨应用泛化，因此需要一种更稳健、更具语义理解能力的方法来解析这些行为数据。

Method: 提出名为WorkflowView的框架，利用大语言模型（LLM）将低级的、有时序戳的交互日志抽象为高级的任务活动。该方法在零样本（Zero-shot）任务描述重建、少样本（Few-shot）学生流失预测以及隐私保护下的AI工具集成分析三个不同领域进行了验证。

Result: 实验表明WorkflowView具有极高的有效性和通用性：在浏览器日志任务中达到0.91的语义相似度；在MOOC日志的学生流失预测中，仅用五个样本即达到了0.90的加权F1分数；并成功实现了在匿名保护下的AI工具工作流分析。

Conclusion: 基于LLM的抽象化方法为将低级行为数据转化为高级、可解释且可操作的洞察提供了一条稳健且高效的路径。该研究强调了在处理复杂交互日志时，利用大模型的语义理解能力超越传统深层模型噪声敏感和泛化能力弱的局限性。同时，研究也指出了在实际应用中必须考虑计算效率和用户隐私保护。

Abstract: Sequential or time-stamped interaction logs provide objective records of digital application usage, yet their granularity and noise often obscure meaningful insights into people's work. Such insights are essential for improving digital products in ways grounded in real-world user interactions. Prior research has applied deep learning models to cluster user actions into high-level activities, but these approaches are highly sensitive to noise and struggle to generalize across applications. To address this limitation, we introduce WorkflowView, a framework that uses large language models (LLMs) to abstract low-level action sequences into high-level activities. We establish the effectiveness and generality of our approach across three distinct, challenging sequential tasks and diverse domains: (a) zero-shot task description reconstruction from browser logs (achieving high semantic similarity, $μ_{sim} = 0.91$), (b) few-shot student dropout prediction using MOOC interaction logs (reaching weighted $F_1 = 0.90$ with only five few-shot examples), and (c) anonymized, privacy-preserving analysis of AI tool integration within document workflows in Microsoft Word. Our work demonstrates that LLM-based abstraction is a robust and efficient path forward for transforming low-level behavioral data into high-level, interpretable, and actionable insights. We also discuss practical considerations for deploying LLM-based inferences within logging infrastructures, including computational efficiency and user privacy.

</details>


### [84] [Towards Direct Latent-Space Synthesis for Parallel Branches in LLM-Agent Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14672)
*Shikun Liu,Mufei Li,Dongqi Fu,Haoyu Wang,Yinglong Xia,Hong Li,Hong Yan,Pan Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 Parallel-Synthesis 框架，通过直接合成并行工作代理产生的 KV cache，而非拼接文本，解决了代理系统并行分支处理的效率瓶颈，在显著降低延迟的同时保持了高质量的合成性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大型语言模型（LLM）作为代理系统执行引擎时，仍通过顺序文本接口处理上下文，这与现代代理工作流（通常涉及并行分支处理、检索和候选生成）存在架构失配。传统的文本拼接方式不仅丢失了并行结构信息，还导致了冗余的预填充（prefill）计算开销。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为 Parallel-Synthesis 的框架，包含两个核心组件：1. Cache Mapper：用于校准来自独立分支的 KV cache，使其能够被统一处理；2. 微调后的 Synthesizer Adapter：使得模型能够直接从非序列化的并行 KV cache 中进行生成。通过专门的训练数据，使合成器学会聚合不同分支的缓存信息，并蒸馏传统文本拼接合成的推理能力。

Result: 在数学、科学问答、代码生成、GAIA 等 9 个下游数据集上，Parallel-Synthesis 在 7 个数据集上持平或优于传统的基于文本拼接的合成方法，且首字延迟（TTFT）降低了 2.5 倍至 11 倍。

Conclusion: Parallel-Synthesis 证明了直接基于 KV cache 进行合成是一种高效且可行的新型接口，为构建原生支持并行代理架构的系统提供了重要范式，能够显著提升代理系统的执行效率与综合能力。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly serve as execution engines for agentic systems, yet they still consume context through a sequential text interface. This creates a mismatch with modern structured agent workflows, in which independent branches explore subtasks, retrieve evidence, or generate candidate solutions before a final synthesis step. Existing systems typically merge these branches by concatenating their textual outputs, which discards the parallel structure and incurs redundant prefill computation. In this work, we introduce Parallel-Synthesis, a plug-and-play framework that enables a synthesizer to directly consume the KV caches produced by parallel worker agents. Parallel-Synthesis combines a cache mapper that calibrates independently generated branch caches with a fine-tuned synthesizer adapter that enables generation from this non-sequential cache interface. We train Parallel-Synthesis using data that exposes the synthesizer to parallel cache contexts, teaches aggregation across cached branches, and distills reasoning behavior from standard text-concatenation-based synthesis. Across nine downstream datasets spanning math, science QA, code generation, GAIA, and multi-agent database diagnosis, Parallel-Synthesis matches or outperforms text-based synthesis on seven datasets and remains close on the other two. It also reduces time-to-first-token by 2.5x-11x, suggesting that direct cache-based synthesis is a promising interface for more native and efficient synthesis over parallel agent branches.

</details>

### [85] [Can Editing 1 Neuron Fix Repetition Loops in LLMs?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13705)
*Aristotelis Lazaridis,Aman Sharma,Dylan Bates,Brian King,Vincent Lu,Jack FitzGerald*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了Gemma 4模型在长文本生成中的“重复循环”病理，发现其可通过定位并修改少量关键神经元权重来消除，但对于因知识匮乏导致的深层“思维循环”，权重编辑手段则无能为力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gemma 4 指令微调模型在处理长篇事实枚举任务时表现出严重的重复崩溃现象（高达95%的重复率），且难以通过提示词工程或采样调整解决。研究者旨在探究这种缺陷是否局限于特定的模型内部参数，并验证是否可以通过最小规模的权重修改来消除这些行为。

Method: 研究团队通过逐层消融（per-layer ablation）和神经元归因（per-neuron attribution）技术，定位导致模型生成重复循环的特定MLP神经元或专家路由。随后，通过静态权重编辑（如神经元抑制或符号反转）对模型进行“手术”，并在完整生成测试中验证该方法的效果，同时在保留通用基准测试得分的前提下评估其可行性。

Result: 研究成功识别并修复了导致重复循环的关键神经元，证明了通过微小权重修改（甚至单个神经元调整）即可消除特定的病理行为。然而，这种编辑手段无法解决模型在长思维预算下因事实知识不足而陷入的“思维循环”困境，表明该问题在根本上是知识精度问题，而非可以通过编辑参数解决的电路错误。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过针对性的权重“手术”可以有效定位并消除模型生成过程中的特定病理行为（如重复循环），但同时也明确了该方法的局限性：权重编辑无法弥补模型缺失的知识。针对长序列推理中的“思维循环（doom loops）”问题，模型表现的根本原因在于知识精度不足，而非单纯的电路故障。

Abstract: Yes. Can it cure doom loops? Probably not.
  The Gemma 4 instruction-tuned models share a reproducible failure: on long factual enumeration prompts, such as listing every episode of a TV series, the 88 IAU constellations, or the 151 original Pokemon, they collapse into repetition, either a tight verbatim loop or a list whose entries decay onto a single answer. These loops occur at rates as high as 95% and survive prompt rewording, inference-engine changes, and most sampling adjustments. In this paper we explore whether this behavior is localized enough to remove by weight edits. To localize the cause, we use per-layer ablation and per-neuron attribution, then confirm the strongest candidates with full-generation sweeps. The loops trace to a small set of MLP neurons (or, in the 26B-A4B Mixture-of-Experts model, a few routed experts) which we suppress with static weight edits. These "surgeries" can be as small as a single sign-inverted neuron (in the E2B model). The size of the effective edits grows with model scale, but in all cases, the loop patterns can be addressed at normal generation budgets while preserving general-purpose benchmark scores. However, the edits do not solve everything: we also study longer thinking budgets, where the two larger models most visibly enter doom looping, i.e. a non-convergent regime in which the model self-corrects in circles over a fact it cannot recall, exhausting the budget without committing to a final answer. We show this residual failure is reduced but not eliminated by the same edits, and argue it is fundamentally a knowledge-precision problem rather than a removable circuit; weight surgery can delete a loop, but it cannot supply a missing fact. Our results are both a feasibility demonstration, that is, evidence that a concrete generation pathology can be localized to a few parameters and edited out, and a delineation of where that approach stops.

</details>


### [86] [Efficient On-Device Diffusion LLM Inference with Mobile NPU](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13740)
*Tuowei Wang,Yanfan Sun,Ju Ren*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: llada.cpp 是首个专门为移动端 NPU 设计的扩散大模型推理框架，通过投机解码、双路径修正和内存优化，在移动设备上实现了高达 42 倍的推理性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散大模型（dLLMs）通过并行去噪加速生成，但在移动端部署时，由于 token 提交导致每块有效负载减少、KV 缓存重用复杂以及 NPU 地址空间限制导致的数据传输开销过大，导致在移动 NPU 上难以高效运行，因此急需一种针对性的推理框架。

Method: 该研究提出了三种核心技术：1. 多块投机解码（Multi-Block Speculative Decoding）：利用后续块的预测填充当前块后期较小的负载；2. 双路径渐进式修正（Dual-Path Progressive Revision）：通过 CPU 处理不稳定的 Token 修正，避免阻塞 NPU 的密集计算；3. 交换优化内存运行时（Swap-Optimized Memory Runtime）：压缩 NPU 可见地址布局，实现数据预取与计算的重叠，降低传输开销。

Result: llada.cpp 在多种硬件平台和 dLLM 工作负载下进行了验证。实验结果表明，该框架在保持生成质量的同时，将 LLaDA-8B 的生成延迟比 CPU 基准（带前缀 KV 缓存重用）降低了 17 倍至 42 倍。

Conclusion: llada.cpp 是首个针对移动端 NPU 优化的扩散大模型（dLLM）推理框架。通过多块投机解码、双路径渐进式修正以及内存运行时优化，该框架有效解决了 NPU 在处理 dLLM 时面临的负载碎片化、缓存管理复杂及数据传输瓶颈等问题，实现了大幅的推理加速。

Abstract: Diffusion large language models (dLLMs) accelerate generation by denoising multiple tokens in parallel, making them attractive for latency-sensitive mobile inference. However, repeated denoising introduces substantial computation on smartphones. Mobile neural processing units (NPUs) offer high-throughput dense matrix computation, but efficiently exploiting them remains challenging: token commitment shrinks per-block effective workloads, token revision complicates KV cache reuse, and limited NPU-visible address space incurs costly remapping and data transfer overheads.
  In this paper, we propose llada.cpp, the first NPU-aware inference framework for accelerating dLLMs on smartphones. llada.cpp aligns block-wise dLLM inference with the execution characteristics of mobile NPUs through three techniques. (1) Multi-Block Speculative Decoding fills the shrinking workload in late-stage current-block decoding with speculative future-block tokens. (2) Dual-Path Progressive Revision keeps committed tokens revisable until stable and refreshes unstable tokens through a CPU-side path without stalling dense NPU execution. (3) Swap-Optimized Memory Runtime compacts NPU-visible address layouts and overlaps data staging with NPU computation to reduce remapping and transfer overheads. We implement llada.cpp as an end-to-end framework and evaluate it across diverse hardware platforms and dLLM workloads. llada.cpp reduces LLaDA-8B generation latency by 17x-42x over the CPU baseline with prefix KV cache reuse, while preserving generation quality.

</details>


### [87] [High-Frequency Pricing at Scale for E-Commerce](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13741)

TL;DR: 针对时尚电商促销场景，本文设计了一种基于梯度提升树预测与多目标优化的定价系统，成功将定价决策从数小时缩短至数分钟，并在大规模实验中实现了约6%的利润增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统时尚电商促销定价系统存在粒度粗（通常为周）、响应慢（决策耗时长）以及难以平衡短期收入与长期利润的局限，无法应对促销期间波动剧烈的需求模式。

Method: 提出了一种“先预测后优化”的定价架构：首先利用梯度提升树（Gradient-boosted trees）进行每日粒度的需求预测，随后通过多目标优化框架，在最大化长期利润和净商品价值（NMV）之间进行权衡。

Result: 在Zalando的12个市场进行了23次A/B测试。结果显示，与原有的半人工半算法系统相比，新系统在保持销售额和营收水平相当的前提下，利润提升了约6%，并将定价决策时间从数小时缩短至数分钟。

Conclusion: 通过“预测-优化”架构在时尚电商促销定价中的成功部署，证明了该方法能够有效解决大规模、高频次定价决策挑战，在提升短期利润的同时兼顾销售额与长期盈利能力。

Abstract: This paper presents the design, development, and implementation of a specialized forecast-then-optimize algorithmic pricing tool for sales campaigns in fashion e-commerce. Sales events present unique challenges for pricing including volatile demand patterns, rapid pricing decisions, and the need to balance short-term revenue with long-term profitability. We describe our approach combining daily-resolution demand forecasting using gradient-boosted trees with a multi-objective optimization framework that maximizes both long-term profit and net merchandise value for more than 5 million articles. Our solution addresses key limitations of existing weekly-granularity systems by implementing a forecast-then-optimize architecture that reduces pricing decision time from hours to minutes. We validate our approach through 23 A/B tests across 12 markets during 2023-2024 sales campaigns at Zalando, one of Europe's leading online fashion retailers. Experimental results demonstrate that the new pricing system achieves approximately 6% higher profit while maintaining equivalent performance on sales and revenue compared to the previous manual-algorithmic hybrid approach. Based on these results, the algorithm was successfully deployed to production and now handles the majority of algorithmic pricing decisions for sales campaigns at the company.

### [88] [A fully GPU-based workflow for building physics emulators of hypersonic flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13742)
*Fabian Paischer,Dylan Rubini,Deniz A. Bezgin,Aaron B. Buhendwa,David Hauser,Florian Sestak,Johannes Brandstetter,Sebastian Kaltenbach,Nikolaus A. Adams*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合可微分流体求解器（JAX-Fluids）与残差细化机制的 GPU 加速框架，旨在解决高超声速流场仿真中传统深度学习模型难以处理激波梯度及物理一致性差的问题，显著提升了代理模型在工程设计中的可靠性与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统降阶模型（ROM）和神经网络模拟器在处理高超声速流场时，难以有效捕捉激波等陡峭梯度，且往往缺乏物理一致性，导致在工业工程应用中难以达到所需的精度与可靠性。因此，需要开发一种既能保持高保真度又具备低计算成本、且物理一致的模拟方案。

Method: 1. 基于 GPU 加速的工作流：利用 JAX-Fluids 可微分高保真流体求解器进行高效数据生成；2. 物理感知细化：通过残差驱动的细化机制（Residual-based refinement）将物理守恒方程纳入神经网络训练，增强模型的物理一致性；3. 模型架构评估：对比了多种神经网络架构，分析了其在高超声速流场预测中的缩放行为与优劣。

Result: 1. 实现了基于 JAX-Fluids 的全 GPU 加速工作流，显著提升了数据集生成与模型训练效率；2. 验证了残差细化方法能够有效降低模型残差，即使在缺乏完整真值数据、仅有网格与输入参数的情况下，也能显著增强预测的物理一致性；3. 证明了集成可微分模拟和残差细化后，生成的物理模拟器在训练分布之外仍能保持良好的可靠性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于可微分求解器与残差细化的框架，成功克服了传统代理模型在处理高超声速流场陡峭梯度时的物理不一致性问题。该工作证明了将物理约束纳入模型训练对于提升 surrogate 模型在分布外场景下的鲁棒性至关重要，为工程设计循环中的快速高保真模拟提供了有效路径。

Abstract: The ability to resolve complex physical phenomena with high fidelity and at low computational cost is central to addressing key challenges in modern engineering. A prime example lies in hypersonic flows, where the precise prediction of the full flowfield topology, in particular with respect to shock wave location and intensity, is critical. Yet supersonic and hypersonic flows continue to be a stumbling block for traditional reduced-order models and neural emulators that struggle to capture steep gradients in flow states with physical consistency in applications of industrial relevance. To that end, we introduce a fully GPU based workflow that integrates accelerated data generation with the training of neural emulators augmented by uncertainty quantification and physics-aware refinement. Our workflow is enabled by a differentiable high-fidelity solver (JAX-Fluids) which we employ for rapid dataset creation and residual-based improvement of the neural emulator to enhance physical consistency. Building on this framework, we first present a suite of model architectures and analyze their scaling behavior to expose their strengths and shortcomings. We then show that residual-based refinement enables training on cases where only mesh and input parameters are available, substantially reducing residuals and improving physical consistency. Together, differentiable simulation and residual-based refinement yield physics emulators that remain reliable beyond their training distribution, a key requirement for deploying surrogates in real-world engineering design loops.

</details>


### [89] [FedSPC: Shared Parameter Correction for Personalized Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13748)
*Kannanthodath Induchoodan Ajay Menon,Christian Prehofer,Yunfei Xu,Toru Hirano*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对个性化联邦学习中共享参数受异构数据干扰的问题，本文提出了 FedSPC 方法，通过对共享参数进行控制变量修正，有效解决了参数更新不一致，并在多个基准测试中显著提升了主流算法的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在个性化联邦学习（PFL）中，共享参数和个性化参数通常被联合训练。然而，不同客户端本地目标函数的差异会导致共享参数在更新时出现不一致，进而削弱共享表征的质量。该研究旨在解决这一优化冲突问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 FedSPC（Federated Shared Parameter Correction）的联邦共享参数修正方法。该方法仅针对个性化联邦学习模型中的共享参数部分应用控制变量法（control-variate correction）进行更新修正，而不干扰个性化参数的训练，具有高度的通用性。

Result: 在 CIFAR-100 和 Tiny-ImageNet 数据集上，基于 ViT、ResNet-34 和 VGG-11 等多种架构的实验表明，FedSPC 能够普遍提升 FedPer、FedRep、FedBABU、LG-FedAvg 和 Ditto 等主流个性化联邦学习方法的性能。

Conclusion: FedSPC 是一种通用的、模块化的修正方法，能够有效解决个性化联邦学习中因本地目标函数差异导致的共享参数更新不一致问题，从而显著提升现有 PFL 方法的性能。

Abstract: Personalized federated learning (PFL) is one of the important approaches in federated learning for addressing statistical heterogeneity while enabling client-specific adaptation. Many PFL methods split the model into shared and personalized parameters, which are jointly trained on each client. However, this creates an optimization issue: shared parameters are updated by clients optimizing different local objectives, which can lead to inconsistent shared updates and weaken the shared representation. To address this problem, we propose Federated Shared Parameter Correction (FedSPC), a modular correction method for PFL. FedSPC applies control-variate correction only to the shared parameters of a given PFL method, while leaving personalized parameters unchanged. It can be integrated into three common PFL settings: shared feature extractors, shared classifiers, and fully shared models with local regularization. Experiments on CIFAR-100 and Tiny-ImageNet with ViT, ResNet-34, and VGG-11 show that FedSPC improves performance across representative PFL methods, including FedPer, FedRep, FedBABU, LG-FedAvg, and Ditto.

</details>


### [90] [The Weight Norm Sets the Grokking Timescale: A Causal Delay Law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13753)
*Truong Xuan Khanh,Doan Hoang Viet,Luu Duc Trung,Phan Thanh Duc*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过实验证明了神经网络的“Grokking”现象（延迟泛化）直接受权重范数动态控制；通过固定权重范数，揭示了泛化延迟与范数之间存在严格的指数关系，并指出LayerNorm通过解耦权重尺度可以改变这一动态过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 关于神经网络中“Grokking”（即模型在训练误差趋于零后，经过长时间训练才出现泛化现象）的成因存在争议，尤其是权重范数在其中的作用尚不明确。研究者旨在通过直接干预权重范数，验证其是否为控制grokking延迟的关键因素。

Method: 研究者采用“干预式”实验方法，在训练过程中强制固定神经网络的权重范数（Clamp the norm），对比在自由训练（free training）条件下的表现。通过调节范数倍数和观察泛化延迟时间（T_grok）的变化，量化两者之间的数学关系，并分析了LayerNorm对这一过程的影响。

Result: 研究发现，在自由训练中，网络在权重范数达到一个临界值Wc时开始泛化；当人为固定权重范数时，泛化延迟时间与范数大小呈指数关系（T_grok ∝ exp(α * ρ)），且该规律在不同模数下具有极高的拟合度。LayerNorm能够通过解耦权重尺度来消除这种延迟依赖，证实了权重范数演化是影响grokking的关键。

Conclusion: Grokking的延迟本质上是由权重范数（Weight Norm）的演变动态驱动的。通过干预实验证实，权重范数与泛化延迟之间存在严格的指数关系，而归一化技术（如LayerNorm）可以通过解耦权重尺度来消除这种依赖，从而揭示了grokking动态背后的控制机制。

Abstract: Grokking is the delayed onset of generalization in neural networks, arising long after they fit the training data. Whether the weight norm causes this delay is disputed: some studies report a critical norm at the transition, others observe grokking with no fixed norm at all. We settle this by intervening on the norm during training rather than only observing it. Under free training with weight decay, networks grok when the weight norm reaches a value Wc that varies little across seeds and learning rates (CV 1 to 2 percent) and grows with the modular base as a power law. When we instead clamp the norm to a fixed multiple rho of Wc and hold it there, the network still groks, but the delay follows T_grok proportional to exp(alpha rho). One exponent, alpha near 7.5, fits this delay across four moduli (R^2 = 0.996). Over the swept ranges the held norm moves the delay by about 19x and the learning rate by only about 2x, and holding the norm above Wc slows grokking rather than preventing it. A final LayerNorm removes the dependence by decoupling weight scale from the network function; without it the exponential law returns. This pinned-norm delay is the exponential counterpart to the logarithmic delay predicted for a freely contracting norm.

</details>


### [91] [D2H-AD: A Hybrid Model Utilizing Hyperdimensional Computing for Advanced Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13754)
*Ghazal Ghajari,Elaheh Ghajari,Ashutosh Ghimire,Saeid Ataei,Faris Alsulami,Fathi Amsaad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为D2H-AD的基于超维计算（HDC）的轻量级异常检测框架，通过集成密度感知编码与距离计算，在边缘设备上实现了比传统深度学习模型更高效、更精准且具备更好可解释性的异常检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的机器学习和深度学习异常检测方法通常依赖大规模标记数据集，计算开销高，且难以在边缘计算环境或高维数据场景下扩展。因此，亟需一种轻量级、可扩展且计算高效的替代方案，以应对资源受限环境下的实时异常检测需求。

Method: 提出了一种名为D2H-AD的新型异常检测框架，该框架基于超维计算（HDC）范式，将信息转化为高维分布式向量。核心创新点在于将基于距离的相似度评估与密度感知编码整合到一个统一的框架中，利用二进制计算实现高效的数据处理。

Result: 实验结果显示，D2H-AD在五个基准数据集上均优于HDAD、ODHD、One-Class SVM、Isolation Forest和Autoencoders等五个基准模型。在ROC-AUC和F1-score指标上表现卓越，同时对类不平衡、噪声和复杂数据具有较强的鲁棒性，且具备内存占用小、延迟低等优势。

Conclusion: D2H-AD框架验证了超维计算（HDC）在异常检测领域的潜力，提供了一种轻量级、高能效且易于解释的解决方案。该方法通过结合距离与密度感知编码，在处理资源受限的边缘计算场景和高维实时数据时，展现出优于传统深度学习和机器学习基准的性能，非常适合TinyML应用。

Abstract: Anomaly detection is a fundamental component of intelligent systems with applications in healthcare, cybersecurity, smart grids, and IoT environments. Although conventional machine learning and deep learning methods have demonstrated effectiveness in identifying anomalies, they often rely on large labeled datasets, incur high computational costs, and face scalability challenges in edge and high-dimensional settings. This paper presents D2H-AD, a novel anomaly detection framework based on Hyperdimensional Computing (HDC), a brain-inspired paradigm that represents information using high-dimensional distributed vectors. Unlike existing HDC-based methods, D2H-AD integrates distance-based similarity and density-aware encoding within a unified framework, improving anomaly representation and detection performance. Ablation studies show that hyperdimensional encoding alone yields up to 5.4% higher ROC-AUC than applying the same density-distance scoring directly in the original feature space. Furthermore, D2H-AD consistently outperforms five established baselines, namely HDAD, ODHD, One-Class SVM, Isolation Forest, and Autoencoders, across all evaluated datasets. The framework is lightweight, interpretable, and computationally efficient, making it suitable for resource-constrained and real-time applications. We validate D2H-AD on five benchmark datasets and demonstrate superior F1-score and ROC-AUC performance, together with robustness to class imbalance, noise, and data complexity. In addition to improved accuracy, D2H-AD offers scalability, a small memory footprint, and low-latency operation enabled by binary computations and a compact design. These properties make it particularly attractive for TinyML and edge AI deployments. The proposed framework highlights the potential of HDC for accurate, interpretable, and energy-efficient anomaly detection in dynamic environments.

### [92] [Beyond LoRA: Is Sparsity-Induced Adaptation Better?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13767)
*Elijah Cadenhead,Cristian McGee,Xin Li,El Houcine Bergou,Aritra Dutta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文深入分析了LoRA类微调方法的泛化性，通过引入稀疏化策略（cLA与c^3LA）进一步压缩了参数空间，在大幅降低显存和计算成本的同时，保持了与现有PEFT方法相当的微调性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨现有低秩自适应（LoRA）及其变体在参数高效微调中的泛化性能差异，并深入研究结构化低秩限制如何影响微调效果，旨在通过引入稀疏性进一步降低微调过程的计算和内存成本。

Method: 提出了Cheap LoRA (cLA) 和 chained circulant variant (c^3LA) 等稀疏化PEFT扩展方法；通过诱导稀疏性将cLA定义为非对称LoRA的结构化实例；推导了这些变体的信息论泛化误差界；并利用损失景观（loss landscapes）和谱分析工具，对11种微调方法在14个数据集上的性能进行了大规模实证评估。

Result: 实验结果显示，cLA等稀疏化方法在保持竞争力的同时，训练时间最高可减少10%，峰值GPU显存占用最高可降低15%。此外，文章提出的理论泛化界比常规分析工具更具一致性和原则性。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论证明与大规模实证分析表明，将LoRA类方法的权重更新限制在稀疏的结构化列空间中，不仅能保持与参数量相当的基准方法相近的性能，还能显著降低训练时间和显存占用，从而为参数高效微调（PEFT）提供了更具成本效益的途径。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation (LoRA) and its variants provide a memory- and compute-efficient alternative to full fine-tuning of pre-trained models. However, questions remain about the comparative generalizability of these approaches and how the structural restrictions on low-rank updates preserve effective adaptation performance. We present a historical framing, covering the past (full fine-tuning and original LoRA), the present (different variants of LoRA), and propose simpler, cheaper, parameter-efficient extensions by inducing sparsity within existing LoRA variants: Cheap LoRA (cLA), training a single low-rank factor with the other fixed (deterministically or, in its randomized variant, stochastically), and the chained circulant variant, ${c}^3$LA. We frame cLA as a structured instance of asymmetric LoRA, serving as a controlled column-subspace restriction of full fine-tuning. We derive information-theoretic generalization error bounds for these variants, marking one of the first endeavors in this area. Empirically, we evaluate 11 fine-tuning methods across 10 pre-trained models and 14 datasets, analyzing the fine-tuned models' performance and generalization using tools such as loss landscapes and spectral analysis. Despite the sensitivity of fine-tuned models to the pre-trained model, datasets, and other factors, our study suggests that restricting LoRA-based PEFT methods' adaptation to a sparse, structured column space remains competitive across tasks with their parameter-matched baselines while reducing up to 10% training time and peak GPU memory up to 15%, even with a naïve, non-optimized, sparse implementation. Our theoretical and empirical generalization measures provide a more consistent and principled approach to their cost-effective adaptation than commonly used analytical tools. Overview and code are available at: https://elicaden.github.io/Beyond_LoRA/.

### [93] [Diffusion Policy Optimization without Drifting Apart](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13795)
*Haozhe Jiang,Haiwen Feng,Pieter Abbeel,Jiantao Jiao,Angjoo Kanazawa,Nika Haghtalab*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对扩散策略强化学习中的不稳定性，该论文提出了DiPOD框架，通过引入在线ELBO正则化来修复由“双重漂移”引起的梯度失配问题，有效提升了训练效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散策略梯度方法在训练中往往不稳定，无法实现可靠的策略改进。研究发现其核心问题在于“双重漂移（double-drift）”现象，即变分代理目标的优化导致ELBO偏离真实的对数似然，进而导致代理策略梯度与期望回报的真实梯度不匹配。

Method: 提出了一种名为DiPOD的扩散策略优化框架。该方法通过在策略改进的梯度更新中交替进行自蒸馏，维持变分下界（ELBO）的紧致性，并在扩散策略梯度更新中引入在线ELBO正则化项，从而对齐代理梯度与真实回报梯度。

Result: 实验结果表明，在扩散语言模型微调和连续控制任务中，DiPOD显著提升了训练的稳定性，并且能够达到比现有方法更高的奖励水平。

Conclusion: DiPOD通过结合自蒸馏机制与策略梯度更新，有效解决了扩散策略强化学习训练中的不稳定性问题，为扩散模型的策略优化提供了一种稳健且通用的解决方案。

Abstract: RL post-training has become increasingly pivotal for improving diffusion policies, but existing diffusion policy-gradient methods are often unstable and cannot achieve reliable policy improvement. We identify the cause as the double-drift phenomenon: optimizing a variational surrogate can let the ELBO separate from the true log-likelihood, which then makes the resulting proxy policy gradient misaligned with the true policy gradient of expected return. We propose \textbf{DiPOD}, a diffusion policy optimization framework that maintains tight-bound behavior throughout training by interleaving self-distillation with policy-improving gradient updates. This leads to a simple and practical algorithm: augmenting each diffusion policy-gradient update with an on-policy ELBO regularizer. Across diffusion language model post-training and continuous-control diffusion policies, DiPOD substantially stabilizes training and reaches higher rewards than previous methods.

</details>


### [94] [Neural Variability Enhances Artificial Network Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13801)
*Robin Preble,Praveen Venkatesh,Stefan Mihalas,Kameron Decker Harris*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在人工神经网络中引入类似生物神经系统的“相关噪声”，发现这种结构化噪声能够显著提升模型应对对抗性攻击及自然图像干扰的鲁棒性，且该方法仅需局部信息即可实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物学研究发现皮层神经元对重复刺激表现出显著的试次间变异性，这可能是有意义的信号而非纯粹的噪声。受此启发，本文旨在探讨在人工神经网络中引入类似的“相关噪声”（Correlated Noise）是否能像在生物系统中那样，增强模型在面对对抗性攻击和自然图像修改时的鲁棒性。

Method: 研究人员通过分析人工神经网络在原始输入和经修改（对抗性攻击或自然噪声干扰）输入下激活值的协方差，探究了结构化噪声对网络鲁棒性的影响。实验重点考察了不同类型的噪声结构在面对不同攻击类型时的泛化能力。

Result: 研究发现，结构化噪声能有效提升网络的鲁棒性。具体而言：1. 结构化噪声对于抵御自然图像修改尤为有效，但这种结构在不同修改类型间的泛化性较差；2. 对抗性攻击产生的噪声结构则表现出更强的跨攻击类型泛化能力。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在人工神经网络中引入结构化噪声能够显著提升模型对对抗性攻击和自然图像修改的鲁棒性。这种策略不仅具有生物学合理性，而且仅依赖局部信息即可实现，为构建更稳健的深度学习模型提供了新的设计思路。

Abstract: Neural responses in cortex exhibit substantial trial-to-trial variability in response to repeated stimuli, while peripheral sensory neurons respond far more consistently, leading many to wonder whether stochasticity may carry meaning. Existing work has argued that noise and signal correlations may be optimized for discrimination in animals, whereas artificial neural network (ANN) studies have shown similar benefits of noise in machine learning tasks, although most ANN work has neglected the effects of correlations. Here we investigate whether correlated noise improves the robustness of artificial neural networks to adversarial attacks and naturalistic image modifications. Using the covariance of activations under modified versus clean inputs, we find that structured noise may significantly improve network robustness. Robustness to naturalistic image modifications benefits most from structure, but this structure transfers poorly across modification types. In contrast, noise structure from adversarial attacks can generalize to other kinds of attacks. These results suggest that structured noise in ANN activations generally improves robustness, establishing a biologically plausible strategy for creating robust artificial neural networks that only relies on local information.

</details>


### [95] [Neural Slack Variables for Shape Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13803)
*Ruben Wiedemann,Antoine Jacquier,Lukas Gonon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出“神经松弛变量”方法，通过引入辅助网络将约束转为回归问题，不仅解决了神经网络难以严格满足单调性和凸性约束的问题，还在金融波动率建模等实际应用中展现了卓越的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多工业和科学应用中，要求神经网络满足单调性或凸性等函数不等式约束。现有的罚函数法或原始-对偶方法在约束满足度上较为脆弱，且通过架构设计强行保证约束的方法往往受限于简单模型，缺乏灵活性。因此，研究者迫切需要一种能够稳健、灵活地实现函数约束的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“神经松弛变量”（Neural Slack Variables）的深度学习方法。该方法引入一个辅助网络，将原始网络的不等式约束转化为一个回归问题。通过将原始网络输出的约束量与辅助网络学习到的有效目标进行耦合，强制实现约束的满足，并保持函数的正则性。

Result: 在密集网格上的单调性和凸性测试中，神经松弛变量方法实现了零违例，优于传统的罚函数和原始-对偶基准方法；同时，该方法成功应用于金融领域的无套利波动率曲面学习，解决了该工业领域的长期难题。

Conclusion: 本文提出的神经松弛变量方法通过辅助网络引导主网络，成功解决了神经网络在单调性和凸性等函数不等式约束下的稳健性难题，为量化金融等需要严格满足约束条件的领域提供了有效的架构解决方案。

Abstract: Enforcing functional inequality constraints such as monotonicity and convexity in neural networks is a fundamental challenge in many industrial and scientific applications. Classical one-sided penalty methods, along with primal-dual methods gated by complementary slackness, provide constraint gradients only at violated locations, resulting in fragile satisfaction. Architectures that guarantee feasibility by construction, on the other hand, remain largely limited to elementary cases and impose additional inductive biases. We introduce neural slack variables, a deep learning native primal-side approach that converts constraint enforcement into a regression problem by coupling the primary network with a jointly learned auxiliary network. The auxiliary network serves as a valid target for the primary network's constraint quantities, inducing feasibility and regularity. Neural slack variables achieve zero measured violations on dense-grid monotonicity and convexity test cases, where penalty and primal-dual baselines leave residual violations, and enable arbitrage-free learning of volatility surfaces, an open industrial challenge in quantitative finance.

</details>


### [96] [Uncertainty Estimation and Generalization Bounds for Modern Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13818)
*Luis A. Ortega*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究旨在通过贝叶斯视角解析深度学习，提出了可扩展的贝叶斯建模方法（如DVIP），并通过结合PAC-Bayesian与大偏差理论，揭示了过参数化神经网络实现优异泛化的内在机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管神经网络在预测性能上表现卓越，但其泛化能力以及量化不确定性的机理尚未得到充分理解。研究旨在通过贝叶斯推断、函数空间建模和大偏差理论的统一视角，深入解析现代深度学习系统的本质机制。

Method: 1. 提出“深度变分隐式过程”（DVIP）：一种可扩展的贝叶斯框架，将隐式过程推广至深层架构。2. 引入两种后处理方法：变分线性化拉普拉斯近似（VaLLA）和固定均值高斯过程（FMGP），旨在为预训练的确定性网络提供校准后的不确定性估计。3. 理论分析：结合PAC-Bayesian学习理论与大偏差理论，构建了一个统一的概率框架，重点研究神经网络中的多样性、平滑性和随机性如何协同作用促进泛化。

Result: 该论文成功实现了深度学习与贝叶斯方法的融合，不仅提供了一套可扩展的高效贝叶斯建模工具（DVIP、VaLLA、FMGP），还从理论上解释了大型过参数化神经网络为何能够保持良好的泛化性能，弥补了深度学习在不确定性量化和理论基础方面的部分缺失。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了贝叶斯框架不仅能够为深度学习提供强大的不确定性量化能力，还为理解过参数化神经网络的泛化机制提供了严谨的理论支撑。通过将现代深度学习方法与经典的概率论工具相结合，研究为构建更可信、更稳健的智能系统开辟了新途径。

Abstract: This thesis investigates how Bayesian principles can deepen our understanding of modern deep learning systems. While neural networks achieve remarkable predictive performance, their ability to generalize and to quantify uncertainty remains only partly understood. This thesis approaches this challenge from both methodological and theoretical angles: unifying Bayesian inference, function-space modeling, and large-deviation theory under a common probabilistic perspective.
  On the methodological side, the thesis introduces the Deep Variational Implicit Process (DVIP), a scalable Bayesian framework that extends implicit processes to deep architectures. Complementing this, two post-hoc methods -- the Variational Linearized Laplace Approximation (VaLLA) and the Fixed-Mean Gaussian Process (FMGP) -- are proposed to equip pretrained deterministic networks with calibrated uncertainty estimates.
  The theoretical contributions focus on one of the central open questions in modern machine learning: why do large, over-parameterized neural networks generalize so well? To address this, the thesis develops a unified probabilistic framework that connects three key mechanisms -- diversity, smoothness, and stochasticity -- within the language of PAC-Bayesian and large-deviation theory.

### [97] [Attention-Based Estimation of the Individual Treatment Benefit Probability under Dose Variation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13821)
*Lev V. Utkin,Andrei V. Konstantinov,Stanislav K. Kogan,Natalya M. Verbova,Maksim I. Goriunov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出Dose-AIPTB框架，通过注意力机制聚合基于协变量相似性构建的伪标签，首次将个体治疗获益概率（IPTB）的估计能力扩展至多离散剂量设置，为个性化精准给药提供了新方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的个体治疗获益概率（IPTB）估计方法主要局限于二元治疗场景，而临床实践中存在大量的剂量调节需求。因此，迫切需要一种能够处理离散剂量变化、为临床决策提供个性化参考的新型估计框架。

Method: 该方法将个体治疗效应（ITE）的正负符号判别转化为二分类问题。首先，利用协变量相似性进行两两比较以构建伪标签；其次，引入注意力机制（或Nadaraya-Watson核回归）对这些伪标签进行聚合。该框架通过这种方式扩展了对多离散剂量级别的支持，超越了传统二元治疗设置的局限。

Result: 通过在合成数据和真实世界数据集上的实验，研究表明Dose-AIPTB框架在处理协变量偏移、不同样本量及异质性结果时表现稳健。实验结果进一步验证了基于注意力机制的聚合方法在性能上始终优于核回归替代方案。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种适用于离散剂量设置的个体治疗获益概率（IPTB）估计框架——Dose-AIPTB。研究证明了通过注意力机制聚合伪标签在处理剂量变化和个体异质性方面的有效性，为实现基于个体获益概率的个性化剂量决策提供了可靠的理论与实践工具。

Abstract: Estimating the probability that a treatment outperforms a control for an individual patient, called the Individual Probability of Treatment Benefit (IPTB), offers a clinically intuitive alternative to population-average metrics. However, existing methods for IPTB estimation are largely confined to binary treatment settings, despite the prevalence of dose-varying interventions in clinical practice. We propose a general framework for IPTB estimation with ordinal outcomes under discrete dose assignments, called Dose-AIPTB (Dose Attention-based IPTB). Our approach recasts the problem as binary classification over the unobserved sign of the individual treatment effect, constructing pseudo-labels from covariate-similar pairwise comparisons and aggregating them via attention mechanisms or Nadaraya-Watson kernel regression. This formulation naturally accommodates multiple discrete dose levels, extending beyond the binary treatment paradigm. Through numerical experiments on real-world and synthetic data under covariate shift, varying sample sizes, and heterogeneous outcomes, we demonstrate that attention-based aggregation consistently outperforms kernel alternatives. The framework provides a foundation for personalized dose selection grounded in individual-level benefit probabilities. Codes implementing the model are publicly available at https://github.com/NTAILab/AIPTBDose.

</details>


### [98] [A Stationarity-and-Coupling Criterion for Training-Free Time-Lagged Spectral Embeddings of Multivariate Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13823)
*Siddharth Pal,Viktoria Rojkova*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需训练的多元时间序列分类方法，并配套了一套“预检”机制，能在部署前科学预判该方法是否有效，从而在计算效率和预测能力之间取得了平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多元时间序列分析往往依赖复杂的深度学习模型，计算开销巨大。作者试图探究无需训练的固定长度描述符在何种条件下有效，并旨在建立一套可证伪的适用性判据，以明确该类简单方法的理论边界和应用场景。

Method: 作者构建了一个基于时间滞后相关矩阵的描述符 $D(τ)$，并通过 Marchenko-Pastur 边缘截断保留信号特征值，利用余弦相似度进行分类。研究者基于平稳高斯 VAR(1) 模型，推导了该描述符的适用性理论，并设计了“预检”流程（包含增强迪基-福勒检验（ADF）和功率基线饱和度检查）来评估数据集是否适合使用该方法。

Result: 实验结果表明，该描述符在满足适用性条件的四个数据集（如 Sleep-EDF, BCI-IV-2a 等）上表现出色，性能可与复杂基线模型媲美，且计算成本极低；而在不满足条件的数据集（如非平稳 ERP 或功率区分明显的财务数据）上，其表现正如理论预测的那样失效。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种无需训练的多元时间序列描述符 $D(τ)$，其核心价值不在于追求极致精度，而在于建立了一套明确的适用性准则。通过“预检”机制，用户可以在部署前判断该方法是否适用，从而避免盲目使用，这种对模型边界的清晰界定对于资源受限场景具有重要意义。

Abstract: We study training-free fixed-length descriptors for multivariate time series and ask not merely whether such a descriptor performs well, but when it can be expected to work at all. Our object of study is $D(τ)$, built from a time-lagged correlation matrix truncated at the Marchenko-Pastur edge so that only signal-bearing eigenvalues survive and classified by cosine similarity to class centroids with zero learned parameters. The central contribution is not the descriptor but a falsifiable applicability criterion for it. Working from a stationary Gaussian VAR(1) model, we argue that $D(τ)$ separates two classes when the signals are approximately stationary and the class information lives in their cross-channel temporal coupling rather than in marginal per-channel power. We derive, semi-formally, three consequences: a distinguishability condition, why the static ($τ=0$) covariance collapses to chance, and why a stationary but power-discriminated paradigm defeats the descriptor. The criterion is operational: a two-part pre-flight test -- an augmented Dickey-Fuller stationarity check and a power-baseline saturation check -- predicts applicability before any training. We validate both halves on a mixed assortment. On four paradigms that satisfy the criterion (Sleep-EDF, BCI-IV-2a, MIT-BIH, ESC-50) the descriptor is competitive with strong baselines at a fraction of their cost, reaching $88.5\pm4.5\%$ under 20-subject leave-one-subject-out on Sleep-EDF on a single CPU thread. On three that violate it -- non-stationary ERPs, and financial-volatility and wearable-stress regimes that are power-discriminated -- it fails exactly as the pre-flight predicts, and these negatives are the more informative half. We are explicit that $D(τ)$ is not the most accurate representation; its value is a compact, training-free embedding whose domain of validity is known in advance.

</details>


### [99] [SuperThoughts: Reasoning Tokens in Superposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13862)
*Zheyang Xiong,Shivam Garg,Max Yu,Vaishnavi Shrivastava,Haoyu Zhao,Anastasios Kyrillidis,Dimitris Papailiopoulos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SuperThoughts提出了一种通过多Token预测来压缩CoT路径的方法，在几乎不损失性能的前提下，通过每步生成两个Token实现了推理速度的显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长思维链（CoT）虽能提升大语言模型的解题能力，但因串行生成导致计算成本高昂。现有在连续隐空间进行推理的方法面临训练不稳定及难以处理复杂长程任务的问题。

Method: 提出SuperThoughts框架：在训练时通过监督机制将连续的CoT Token对压缩为单个潜在表示，并利用轻量级的多Token预测（MTP）模块在推理时每步解码两个Token；引入基于置信度的自适应回退机制，在模型不确定时切换回标准解码方式。

Result: 在Qwen2.5系列模型上进行测试，在MATH500、AMC等基准测试中，SuperThoughts实现了约20%-30%的思维链长度压缩，推理吞吐量翻倍，且在模型准确率上仅有1-2个百分点的微小下降。

Conclusion: SuperThoughts通过多Token预测机制有效提升了推理效率，证明了在保持高性能的同时，通过压缩推理路径实现长思维链加速是可行的，为大语言模型的高效推理提供了新方向。

Abstract: Long Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning improves LLM problem-solving but is computationally expensive due to sequential token generation. While recent works explore reasoning in continuous latent spaces to bypass discrete token generation, they often struggle with training stability and fail to scale to complex, long-horizon tasks due to lack of supervision signal. We propose SuperThoughts, which compresses pairs of consecutive CoT tokens into single latent representations and decodes two tokens per step via a lightweight Multi-Token Prediction (MTP) module. This preserves discrete token supervision at training time while doubling throughput at inference time. We finetune Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B-Instruct, Qwen2.5-Math-7B-Instruct, Qwen2.5-Math-14B-Instruct, and evaluate on MATH500, AMC, OlympiadBench, and GPQA-Diamond. With a confidence-based adaptive mechanism that falls back to standard decoding when uncertain, SuperThoughts achieves $\sim$20--30\% CoT length reduction while maintaining accuracy with minimal degradation (1-2 points accuracy drop on most tasks).

### [100] [Muon$^p$: Muon with Fractional Spectral Powers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13867)
*Yihe Dong,Will Sawin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究提出了一种名为 Muon^p 的新型优化器，通过在梯度矩阵中引入分数谱幂次，在保持 Muon 原有高效矩阵计算结构的同时，有效利用奇异值信息，显著提升了大规模模型的微调性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Muon 优化器通过将梯度展平（即替换为极因子 $UV^\top$）在训练中表现优异，但这种“完全展平”丢失了对模型微调至关重要的奇异值信息。因此，研究者旨在开发一种方法，既能保留 Muon 的高效矩阵操作，又能通过引入部分谱信息提升微调性能。

Method: 1. 提出 Muon^p 优化器，通过 fractional spectral-power（分数谱幂）$US^pV^\top$ 对梯度进行处理，其中 $p \in (0, 1)$。
2. 证明了分数谱幂无法通过固定的单变量多项式迭代计算。
3. 推导出低阶奇数双变量递归算法，利用矩阵乘法近似计算 $US^pV^\top$，从而保持了 Muon 的计算复杂度和仅矩阵乘法的结构优势。
4. 从 Schatten q-norm 角度分析其理论收敛特性。

Result: 1. 理论上，Muon^p 能够最大化在 Schatten q-norm 下的线性损失改善。
2. 实验表明，在十亿参数规模的模型微调中，Muon^p 在验证困惑度（Perplexity）及下游任务表现上均优于原始的 Muon 算法。
3. 通过谱几何视角分析了 Muon^p 的适用场景，揭示了何时保留奇异谱信息能带来显著增益。

Conclusion: Muon^p 是一种更具灵活性和适应性的优化器，通过引入分数谱幂次，在完全展平（Muon）和梯度下降之间实现了平衡。该研究为理解谱信息如何影响模型适应性提供了理论框架，并证明了在保留部分奇异值信息的情况下，可以显著提升大规模模型的微调效果。

Abstract: Muon is an increasingly widely used optimizer that replaces a gradient $G=USV^\top$ with its polar factor $UV^\top$, thereby flattening the singular spectrum. However, full flattening discards singular-value information that may matter for adaptation. We introduce Muon$^p$, a Muon-style optimizer that instead uses fractional spectral-power updates $US^pV^\top$ for rational $p\in(0,1)$, interpolating between Muon and gradient descent. To make it practical, we prove that fractional spectral powers cannot be computed by any fixed univariate polynomial iteration, and furthermore derive low-degree odd bivariate recurrences that approximate $US^pV^\top$ using only matrix multiplications, preserving Muon's matrix-multiplication-only structure and compute complexity. We show that Muon$^p$ maximizes the linear improvement in loss under the Schatten $q$-norm for $q=1+\frac{1}{p}$. Empirically, Muon$^p$ is especially effective for finetuning: on billion-scale models, Muon$^p$ improves validation perplexity and downstream task performance. We further analyze when Muon$^p$ is less suitable, through the lens of spectral geometry. Our results reveal important insights on when preserving the singular spectrum can bring significant gains, and introduce a principled way to achieve them.

</details>


### [101] [Natively Unlearnable Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13873)
*Gaurav R. Ghosal,Pratyush Maini,Aditi Raghunathan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: NULLs 是一种新型大语言模型架构，通过将模型参数解耦为“共享骨干”和“来源特异性汇”，实现了高效、鲁棒且无需二次训练的机器遗忘，同时保留了联合学习的性能优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模型遗忘技术难以在移除特定训练数据影响的同时，保持模型在联合学习中的性能，因为不同数据源的贡献在模型参数中是高度纠缠的。研究旨在解决如何实现“源级别遗忘”且不牺牲联合学习带来的性能增益。

Method: 提出了一种名为 NULLs（原生不可学习 LLM）的模型类，通过在训练过程中结合共享的“骨干神经元”（Backbone Neurons）和一组稀疏激活的“汇”（Sinks）。训练时，共享知识积累在骨干中，而特定来源知识自然地集中在对应的“汇”中。在遗忘时，只需禁用特定来源的“汇”，无需梯度更新，也无需原始数据。

Result: 在维基百科约600万篇文章的规模下，NULLs 能有效隔离并遗忘单篇文章的特定知识，同时保留语义相关的事实，效果接近重新训练。在哈利波特书籍的案例中，该方法表现出抗对抗提取和抗重学习的鲁棒性，且在下游任务中保持了与标准 Transformer 相当的语言能力。

Conclusion: NULLs 证明了通过在模型架构层面引入源特异性组件，可以实现高效、可靠且无需重新训练的机器遗忘，同时保持模型在联合学习下的强大性能。这表明遗忘机制可以作为大语言模型训练的原生设计，而非事后补救措施。

Abstract: Unlearning aims to remove the influence of specific training data sources, but this has proved challenging because the contributions of different sources are entangled within the model. Isolating source contributions to disjoint parameters makes removal easier, though it obstructs joint learning across sources. We propose NULLs (Natively Unlearnable LLMs), a model class that satisfies the two opposing goals of isolating source-specific contributions and learning jointly across sources, by training a set of shared backbone neurons alongside a pool of sparsely activated sinks. During training, information specific to a source naturally concentrates in its sinks while information shared across sources accumulates in the backbone. A source is then unlearned at deployment by disabling its corresponding sinks, with no gradient updates and no access to the retained data. We show that NULLs scales to Wikipedia's ~6M articles, isolating each as an independent source. Unlearning a single article removes knowledge specific to it while preserving facts shared with semantically related articles, closely matching retraining from scratch. We note that unlearning with NULLs is also robust: in a case study of unlearning the Harry Potter books, NULLs resists both adversarial extraction and relearning that reverses post-hoc unlearning. Finally, NULLs preserves general language capabilities, matching a standard transformer on downstream benchmarks. Together, these results suggest that source-level unlearning need not be an afterthought. It can be built natively into LLM training while retaining the benefits of shared representation learning.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Accurate estimation of long-term care transition probabilities is central to disability insurance pricing, reserving, and solvency assessment. Classical actuarial multi-state models commonly rely on Markov, semi-Markov, or proportional-hazard specifications, which provide a direct connection to cohort projection but may be restrictive for irregular longitudinal health data with nonlinear aging patterns and heterogeneous covariate histories. This paper develops a well-calibrated estimator of multi-state transition probabilities for irregular longitudinal health data. The model learns from individual health history, incorporates the time elapsed between observations, and conditions transition probabilities on demographic and socioeconomic attributes. It produces a valid probability distribution over the next observed health state, with four possible states: healthy, mild disability, severe disability, and death. Individual probabilities are aggregated by age group and origin state to form transition matrices compatible with actuarial cohort projection. Using longitudinal data from the Health and Retirement Study, we compare the proposed estimator with logistic regression, gradient-boosted trees, a recurrent neural network, and a last-state persistence benchmark. The evaluation considers probabilistic accuracy, endpoint discrimination and calibration for severe disability and death, risk concentration, and transition matrix error after aggregation. The proposed estimator improves severe disability discrimination relative to logistic regression and gradient-boosted tree benchmarks, maintains strong calibration, and yields the lowest transition matrix error among the evaluated models in the held-out test analysis. Results show that a structured machine learning estimator can support long-term care transition modeling when judged by calibration and projection fidelity, beyond discrimination.

### [103] [Gefen: Optimized Stochastic Optimizer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13894)
*Nadav Benedek,Tomer Koren,Ohad Fried*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Gefen 是一种内存高效的优化器，通过自动参数块二阶矩共享和一阶矩量化，在不损失性能的前提下，将 AdamW 的优化器内存需求降低了 8 倍，有效提升了大规模模型训练的吞吐量和容量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AdamW 优化器在现代深度学习中应用广泛，但其一阶和二阶矩状态会消耗大量内存（每个参数额外占用两个缓冲区）。为了解决在大规模模型训练中内存受限的问题，作者旨在开发一种能够在保持 AdamW 性能的前提下，显著降低优化器内存占用的方法。

Method: 1. 参数块共享：基于 Hessian 的理论分析，通过初始梯度估计自动划分参数块，共享二阶矩估计；2. 量化处理：利用基于直方图的动态规划算法学习一阶矩的量化码本；3. 系统优化：实现融合 CUDA 内核，无需额外的超参数，与 AdamW 的配置保持一致。

Result: 1. 内存节省：将 AdamW 的优化器内存占用减少了约 8 倍（每十亿参数节省 6.5 GiB）；2. 性能一致性：在多种实验中保持了与 AdamW 相当的收敛性能；3. 训练提升：在 FSDP 和 DDP 设置中，通过减少内存开销支持更大的微批次（microbatch），从而显著提高了训练吞吐量。

Conclusion: Gefen 是一种高效的 AdamW 替代方案，通过创新的参数块共享和动态量化技术，显著降低了内存占用，同时保持了与 AdamW 相当的训练性能。它作为一种即插即用的优化器，在提升训练吞吐量和支持更大模型训练方面具有显著优势。

Abstract: AdamW is a default optimizer for modern deep learning, but its first and second moment states add roughly two parameter-sized buffers to training memory. We propose Gefen, a memory-efficient optimizer that automatically shares second-moment estimates across parameter blocks and quantizes the first moment using a learned codebook, thereby reducing AdamW's memory footprint by ~8x while maintaining the same performance, corresponding to a reduction of 6.5 GiB per billion parameters. The method is motivated by a theoretical result showing that large mixed Hessian entries constrain the ratio of squared gradients toward one, suggesting that Hessian-aligned parameters are natural candidates for sharing second-moment statistics. Since computing Hessians is impractical at scale, Gefen infers block structure from the initial squared gradients, requiring no architecture-specific metadata or hyperparameters beyond AdamW defaults. Gefen learns an exact histogram-based dynamic-programming quantization codebook and reuses the same blocks for first-moment scaling. Across diverse experiments, Gefen achieves the lowest peak optimizer memory among the compared AdamW-like methods while maintaining AdamW-level performance. In FSDP and DDP training, the reduced memory footprint enables larger microbatches and improves throughput significantly over AdamW, providing a practical drop-in replacement with lower memory usage that can increase throughput and enable training larger models or using larger batch sizes. We provide the complete Python implementation, including fused CUDA kernels at https://github.com/ndvbd/Gefen

</details>


### [104] [SpikF-GO: Spiking Fourier Graph Operators for Multivariate Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13901)
*Jafar Bakhshaliyev,Niels Landwehr*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SpikF-GO 是一种新型脉冲图神经网络，通过在脉冲域引入图建模与傅里叶谱处理，有效解决了多变量时间序列预测中的变量依赖建模难题，在实现高预测精度的同时大幅降低了能耗。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 SpikF-GO 模型，核心包含：1. 将多变量时间序列构建为图结构，以捕捉变量间相关性；2. 引入基于尖峰的谱处理技术；3. 设计“硬具体频率门”（Hard Concrete frequency gate）实现稀疏频率选择；4. 开发“复数 LIF 门”（Complex LIF gate）处理傅里叶分量；5. 可选集成基于中枢模式发生器（CPG）的位置编码以增强长程时间建模。

Conclusion: SpikF-GO 通过将图神经网络与脉冲神经网络有效结合，解决了现有脉冲神经网络在多变量时间序列预测中缺乏变量间依赖建模的问题。该方法在保持低能耗优势的同时，实现了优于现有脉冲神经网络方法及部分人工神经网络基准的性能，证明了基于脉冲的图处理在时间序列任务中的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Spiking Neural Networks (SNNs) have emerged as an energy-efficient alternative to conventional neural networks, demonstrating strong performance in computer vision and robotics. More recently, SNNs have been applied to time series forecasting (TSF), with methods exploring spiking temporal backbones, spike-compatible positional encodings, Fourier-domain processing, and redesigned neuron dynamics. However, existing SNN forecasting approaches process variables independently, lacking explicit mechanisms for modeling inter-variable dependencies. This is a critical limitation in multivariate settings, where cross-variable correlations carry substantial predictive information. We propose Spiking Fourier Graph Operators (SpikF-GO), which addresses this gap by combining a hypervariate graph formulation in which every scalar observation becomes a graph node with spike-driven spectral processing. SpikF-GO introduces a Hard Concrete frequency gate for learnable sparse frequency selection and a Complex LIF gate that applies independent spiking neurons to real and imaginary Fourier components, preserving binary, event-driven computation throughout the spectral domain. We further present a variant incorporating Central Pattern Generator-based positional encodings for stronger long-range temporal modeling. Evaluated on eight benchmarks under a unified experimental protocol, SpikF-GO achieves the best average rank among all SNN methods and outperforms its ANN counterpart, FourierGNN, at reduced energy cost. SpikF-GO maintains competitive accuracy even at substantially smaller embedding dimensions, thereby achieving significant energy reductions. To our knowledge, this is among the first works to bring graph-based multivariate modeling into the spiking domain for TSF and the first to provide a unified comparison across SNN forecasting architectures under a common experimental protocol.

### [105] [Smoothing Dark Areas in Molecular Latent Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13955)
*Xi Wang,Jiahan Li,Yuxuan Xia,Yingcheng Wu,Shaoyi Zheng,Shengjie Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TopVAE 通过优化 VAE 的解码器训练，消除了分子潜在空间中的“暗区”，显著提升了 3D 分子生成的化学质量与生成效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的分子 VAE 主要基于重构目标进行训练，无法保证潜在空间的平滑性和可导航性，导致在扩散采样过程中容易进入解码出无效分子的“暗区”。分子生成对结构和化学精度的要求极高，现有的框架难以胜任。

Method: 提出 TopVAE，这是一种拓扑优化的变分自编码器（VAE）。它在训练过程中通过约束机制强制解码器学习分子的结构和化学规则，从而消除潜在空间中解码出化学无效分子的“暗区”。将 TopVAE 与标准的扩散 Transformer (DiT) 结合使用。

Result: TopVAE 极大地增强了模型在训练分布之外（off-posterior）的鲁棒性。在 QM9 数据集上 FCD-3D 降低了 77%，并获得了最高的有效性和化学正确性（V&C）；在 GEOM-Drugs 数据集上 FCD-3D 降低了 52%；在零样本支架填充任务中，生成分子的稳定性和连通性提升了 1.29 倍。

Conclusion: TopVAE 通过将结构和化学约束内化到解码器训练中，成功解决了潜在空间中的“暗区”问题，显著提升了分子生成的有效性和鲁棒性，为高质量 3D 分子生成提供了更强大的基础框架。

Abstract: Latent diffusion is a promising framework for scalable 3D molecular generation, but it requires a latent space that remains smooth, valid, and navigable beyond posterior samples. Existing molecular VAEs, however, are typically learned through reconstruction-based objectives, which do not guarantee such a latent space. We show that this leads to dark areas: regions of latent space that are reachable during diffusion sampling but decode to disconnected or chemically invalid molecules. Unlike in image generation, molecular decoding requires strict structural and chemical precision, so even small latent perturbations can produce catastrophic failures. We therefore propose TopVAE, a topology-optimized VAE that reduces dark areas by making the decoder internalize structural and chemical constraints during training, eliminating the need for test-time chemical correction. TopVAE greatly improves off-posterior robustness, and when paired with a standard DiT, achieves $77\%$ lower FCD-3D on QM9, the highest V&C, $52\%$ lower FCD-3D on GEOM-Drugs, and $1.29{\times}$ more stable and connected molecules on zero-shot scaffold inpainting.

</details>


### [106] [Can Machine Learning Forecast Rice Yields in Data-Constrained Settings? Satellite Climate Data, National Crop Statistics, and Lessons from Sierra Leone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13959)
*Ibrahim Denis Fofanah*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究首次利用机器学习评估了塞拉利昂水稻产量的可预测性。结果显示，融合气候卫星数据的模型能有效利用早期降雨量实现产量预警，从而为塞拉利昂的农业政策制定提供了可行的量化决策支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 塞拉利昂的农业缺乏数据驱动的决策支持，且此前尚无关于该国作物产量的机器学习研究。研究旨在探究利用现有数据（包括历史统计数据和卫星气候数据）是否能够有效预测水稻产量，以填补农业政策制定的数据空白。

Method: 研究采用了XGBoost、梯度提升决策树（Gradient Boosting）和随机森林（Random Forest）等机器学习算法。评估过程严格遵循防数据泄露协议，采用扩展窗口滚动预测（expanding-window walk-forward evaluation）并在七个留出测试年份进行验证，并与朴素持久性模型进行了基准对比。此外，研究还融合了CHIRPS降雨量和NASA POWER温度等免费卫星气候数据。

Result: 仅使用作物历史统计数据训练的模型表现不佳，无法超越朴素基准。但加入卫星气候数据后，预测误差显著降低，其中XGBoost模型将RMSE从428 kg/ha降低至284 kg/ha。研究发现5月至6月的早期降雨量是影响产量的核心预测因子，该模型能提前数月识别季节性产量风险，但无法预测2018年因机构因素导致的产量崩盘。

Conclusion: 基于气候数据的机器学习模型能够显著提高塞拉利昂水稻产量的预测精度，特别是利用早期降雨量作为关键指标。然而，单一依赖作物历史统计数据无法提供有效的预测，且非气候因素（如制度性问题）导致的产量剧变仍难以预测。研究建议将这些气候感知预测模型纳入国家的农业决策支持系统。

Abstract: Sierra Leone's agriculture operates with almost no data-driven decision support, and no published machine learning study has examined the country's crop yields. We ask whether rice yield can be forecast from data Sierra Leone currently has. Using 25 years of FAOSTAT production data (2000-2024) for nine major crops, we train XGBoost, Gradient Boosting, and Random Forest under a strict anti-leakage protocol with expanding-window walk-forward evaluation across seven held-out years, benchmarked against naive persistence. No model trained on crop statistics alone outperforms persistence. Augmenting with free satellite climate data (CHIRPS rainfall, NASA POWER temperature) reverses this result: a climate-only XGBoost reduces forecast error by one third (RMSE 284 vs 428 kg/ha), a gain that holds for a linear model and is robust to excluding the anomalous 2018 season. Early-season (May-June) rainfall is the dominant predictor, implying seasonal yield risk is observable months before harvest. No model anticipated the 2018 collapse, whose origins were institutional rather than climatic. We translate the findings into policy recommendations for Sierra Leone's Feed Salone Strategy, with a fully open-source pipeline.

### [107] [PostDeg: Placement Beats Parameterization in LayerNorm GNNs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14022)
*Yash Tomar,Aryav Das*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了LayerNorm导致GNN拓扑信息丢失的原因在于其位置安排，并提出了一种简单有效的“后LayerNorm缩放”策略（PostDeg），在不引入额外参数的情况下显著提升了模型在节点选择任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于LayerNorm的图神经网络（GNNs）在处理节点选择任务（如影响力最大化、网络拆解等）时，往往会抹除依赖于节点度、中心性等拓扑信号，本文旨在找出这种信息抹除发生在残差块的哪个具体位置，并提出改进方案。

Method: 通过理论推导分析LayerNorm如何消除节点拓扑信号，指出在LayerNorm之前插入缩放因子会被抵消，而放置在之后则可保留信息。由此提出了一种无参数的后LayerNorm逆度缩放方法（PostDeg），并通过四种“证伪实验”（falsifiers）验证了该设计的有效性与普适性。

Result: 实验表明，PostDeg相比于基准LayerNorm架构，在影响力最大化、网络拆解和最大独立集任务上分别提升了3.5%、2.5%和5.6%，且在所有任务中均取得全胜，通过了所有的证伪性测试。

Conclusion: 拓扑信息的丢失主要归因于LayerNorm在残差块中的放置位置。将标量缩放放置在LayerNorm之后可以有效地保留拓扑信息，这种简单的位置调整优于参数化的复杂度，具有良好的泛化能力。

Abstract: LayerNorm-based GNNs routinely erase the topology signals (degree, centrality, $k$-core) that node-selection policies should depend on, but the literature has not located where in the residual block the erasure happens. We answer that question: a positive per-node scalar inserted before LayerNorm is divided out up to a stabilizer term, while the same scalar inserted after LayerNorm reaches the score head as representation magnitude. The surviving slot is the post-LayerNorm position. We instantiate it with PostDeg, a parameter-free post-LayerNorm inverse-degree scale, and pre-register four falsifiers (graphwise scalars, extra LayerNorm, expressive same-slot capacity, backbone-agnostic source) that would reject the rule. PostDeg gains $+3.5\%/+2.5\%/+5.6\%$ over the LN backbone on influence maximization, network dismantling, and maximum independent set, with $10/10$ paired-seed wins per task; none of the four falsifiers fires. The takeaway is that placement, not parameterization, carries the gain -- a small invariance check that generalizes to any positive topology scalar in any normalized residual stack.

### [108] [Utility-Constrained Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14029)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了一种适用于效用约束马尔可夫决策过程（UCMDPs）的方法，该方法通过风险敏感约束代替传统的风险中性约束，并且无需在训练前预先固定约束限制，允许在训练后对约束范围进行灵活调整。

Abstract: Constrained MDPs (CMDPs) are a widely adopted framework for incorporating safety into RL agents; however, the framework does not support risk-sensitive constraints. This can be problematic: For example, CMDPs allow for optimal solutions that, in order to satisfy the risk-neutral constraints, mix infrequent catastrophic behaviors and frequent, overly conservative ones. Moreover, prior empirical results suggest that enforcing stricter, risk-sensitive constraints can improve performance even under risk-neutral evaluation. The natural framework to incorporate risk-sensitive constraints is utility-constrained MDPs (UCMDPs), but no practical solutions for this problem existed. In this work, we introduce a simple yet powerful methodology for UCMDPs and constrained RL. Besides allowing for risk-sensitive constraints, our framework does not require us to fix constraint limits in advance of training the agent, provided that a sensible range is known. This increases policy flexibility and, in practice, allows for adjustments to these limits at no extra training cost. Besides benefiting from the generality of the framework, our agent shows strong performance in practice, consistently matching or outperforming existing baselines in several Safety Gymnasium benchmark tasks.

### [109] [Decompose Sparsely Where You Should, Absorb Densely Where You Should No](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14040)
*Ruixuan Deng,Zehao Jin,Zekun Wang,Zihan Dong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究发现大模型激活空间中存在无法被稀疏字典有效编码的“计算骨架”。通过在SAE中增加低秩瓶颈，研究证明了该稠密成分对模型计算至关重要，揭示了当前稀疏化解释性方法的局限性，并建议重新审视仅依赖稀疏性进行模型理解的范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统稀疏自编码器（SAE）假设所有的激活内容均可分解为稀疏且单语义的特征。然而，研究者观察到SAE训练中始终存在顽固的“稠密潜变量”，并怀疑激活内容中存在本质上不适合稀疏表示但对模型计算至关重要的低秩、稠密成分。研究旨在验证这一假设并探索如何更好地区分稀疏与稠密特征。

Method: 作者提出了在现有稀疏自编码器（如BatchTopK和Matryoshka）架构中并行加入一个低秩（rank-$r$）线性瓶颈层的方法。该瓶颈层旨在先吸收残差流中的稠密结构，从而减轻稀疏字典试图建模这些不可压缩信息的压力，进而对比分析引入该瓶颈前后的模型性能、稀疏特征的可解释性及因果作用。

Result: 在Gemma-2-2B模型上，实验表明引入rank-24的瓶颈层可减少84%的稠密潜变量，并提升了稀疏探测的准确性。该“计算骨架”被证明在因果上具有高度必要性（移除它会导致模型性能剧烈下降），且与传统的稀疏特征相比，它能更高效地编码语义信息，证实了标准稀疏字典在处理该部分内容时的无效性。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了模型残差流中存在一个无法被稀疏自编码器（SAE）有效建模的“计算骨架”（computational scaffold）。该骨架具有低秩、稠密且在因果上至关重要的特征，现有的稀疏解释性方法在处理该部分时效率低下。这一发现表明，稀疏字典并非全能，未来的可解释性研究应更加关注并显式地建模这种非稀疏的稠密结构。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) are typically trained to reconstruct the \textbf{entire} residual stream through a sparse dictionary, implicitly assuming that all activation content is amenable to sparse, monosemantic decomposition. We question this assumption and hypothesize that activations contain a low-rank, dense component that is computationally important to the model yet inherently unsuitable for sparse representation, which serves as a major source of the persistent dense latents widely observed in trained SAEs. To test this, we add a small rank-$r$ linear bottleneck in parallel with standard SAEs (BatchTopK and Matryoshka), allowing dense structure to be absorbed before sparse reconstruction. On Gemma-2-2B layer 12, a rank-24 bottleneck reduces dense latent count by up to 84\% while improving sparse probing and targeted probe perturbation on both architectures at matched sparsity. The absorbed component is (i) \textbf{structurally identifiable} as the top principal components and outlier dimensions; (ii) \textbf{causally necessary}, with removing it raising next-token cross-entropy by 7.5$\times$, far exceeding the 2.8$\times$ from removing the geometrically near-identical top-24 PCA directions; and (iii) \textbf{redundantly encoded by sparse dictionaries}, with ablating 787 maximally aligned sparse features raising cross-entropy by only 2.9$\times$ and ablating 2,048 topic-aligned features leaving MMLU topic classification virtually unchanged, whereas removing the scaffold drops it from 98.7\% to chance. Together, our findings identify a compact, semantically informative and causally important component of residual stream activations (which we term a \textbf{computational scaffold}) that standard sparse dictionaries represent inefficiently, suggesting that the scope of sparsity-based interpretability methods warrants careful re-examination.

### [110] [Non-Parametric Machine Text Detection via Multi-View Gaussian Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14060)
*Aleem Khan,Nicholas Andrews*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多视角非参数化检测框架，通过融合多种互补特征并使用高斯过程集成，有效提升了机器文本检测器在对抗性攻击下的鲁棒性，并解决了传统分类器在分布偏移下的性能退化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器学习文本检测器在面对改写（paraphrasing）或目标风格迁移等对抗性攻击时性能显著下降。此外，现有的参数化分类器在遇到未见过的攻击或模型时容易做出错误且自信的预测。因此，需要一种能够抵御多种攻击并具备校准不确定性能力的稳健检测机制。

Method: 该方法采用多视角非参数化框架，从单一文档中提取多种互补特征（如风格、似然度、排序特征及结构特征），并利用高斯过程集成（Gaussian process ensemble）对各视角的证据进行聚合，而非依赖易受分布偏移影响的参数化分类器。

Result: 在包括DetectRL、RAID以及PAN2025在内的三个基准测试中，该方法表现出色。实验结果证明，其在面对多种对抗性攻击时，性能优于现有的其他检测方法，且在处理分布外数据时能够提供更可信的概率估计。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于高斯过程集成的多视角非参数化检测框架。通过整合文档的多种互补特征，该方法显著提高了对对抗性攻击的鲁棒性，并在面对分布外输入时具备更好的校准概率和拒识能力，为高风险环境下的文本检测提供了更可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: Adversarial conditions such as paraphrasing and targeted style transfer sharply degrade the accuracy of machine text detectors. A document, however, carries multiple complementary signals (e.g., stylistic features, likelihood and rank-order features, and structural features), and an attack that suppresses one may leave others intact. While a parametric classifier can learn to combine these features given sufficient supervision, classifiers are prone to making confidently incorrect predictions when the distribution shifts (e.g., novel attacks or unseen language models). To address this, we propose a multi-view, non-parametric detection framework that extracts complementary feature views from the same document and aggregates per-view evidence through a Gaussian process ensemble. By aggregating evidence across views, an adversary must simultaneously defeat multiple independent axes of detection, substantially raising the cost of evasion. The Gaussian process formulation additionally provides calibrated probabilities and principled abstention on out-of-distribution inputs, supporting reliable deployment in high-stakes settings. We evaluate on three benchmarks spanning diverse generators and attacks: the DetectRL and RAID benchmarks, and the PAN2025 shared task and demonstrate that our multi-view detector maintains strong performance under the considered attacks, outperforming existing approaches against held out attacks.

### [111] [Rethinking Backdoor Adversarial Unlearning through the Lens of Catastrophic Forgetting in Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14078)
*Zhenqian Zhu,Yamin Hu,Yujiang Liu,Luping Wei,Wenbo Hou,Bin Li,Haodong Li,Wenjian Luo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于连续学习视角和盲反转策略的后门遗忘方法（BI-BAU），通过利用灾难性遗忘机制和期望最大化算法，能够彻底消除模型中存在的各类后门影响，并具有广泛的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的后门防御手段鲁棒性不足，且主流的安全微调策略往往只能提供表面的安全保护，无法彻底根除模型中存在的后门效应，这对于预训练模型的实际部署构成了严峻的安全挑战。

Method: 提出了一种名为“盲反转-后门对抗性遗忘（BI-BAU）”的框架。该方法将后门学习与遗忘建模为连续的三阶段过程，利用灾难性遗忘的机制来推导完全遗忘的必要条件，并通过将双层优化过程集成到期望最大化（EM）算法中，将满足遗忘条件的对抗样本生成问题转化为一个盲反转优化问题（最大后验估计，MAP）。

Result: 实验结果表明，BI-BAU方法能够广泛适用于多种后门攻击，并能有效地从后门模型中彻底消除后门影响。此外，该方法还成功扩展到了未知目标类别的无目标对抗场景及多模态对比学习任务中，验证了其在实际应用场景中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过将后门清理重新定义为一个连续的三个阶段过程，并利用灾难性遗忘机制，成功地从被感染的模型中彻底消除了后门影响。该方法在多种攻击类型和任务场景中表现出高度的普适性和鲁棒性，为解决深度学习模型的安全隐患提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Existing studies reveal that current backdoor defenses exhibit limited robustness and often fail against specific types of attacks. More concerningly, prevailing safety tuning strategies tend to provide only superficial safety protection, as they fall short of completely eliminating the backdoor effects. In this work, we present a novel formulation of backdoor learning and unlearning as a sequential, three-stage process from a continual learning perspective. Within this framework, we formally define complete backdoor unlearning and further derive the necessary conditions for achieving it based on the mechanism of catastrophic forgetting. Guided by these insights, we propose Blind Inversion-Backdoor Adversarial Unlearning (BI-BAU), which formulates the generation of adversarial examples satisfying the unlearning conditions as a blind inversion problem. We solve this by integrating the bi-level optimization process of adversarial training into an Expectation-Maximization (EM) algorithm framework to optimize the maximum a posteriori (MAP) objective. Furthermore, BI-BAU is extended to untargeted adversarial scenarios with unknown target classes, as well as to multi-modal contrastive learning tasks, enhancing its applicability to real-world deployment scenarios where pre-trained models may be compromised. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method exhibits general applicability across a wide spectrum of backdoor attacks and can effectively and thoroughly eliminate the backdoor effects from a backdoor model.

### [112] [Deep Spectral Learning of Embedded Latent Transfer Operators for Stochastic Dynamical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14079)
*Ryogo Tanaka,Yoshinobu Kawahara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为深度谱编码器（DSE）的算子基潜状态空间模型，通过结合深度神经网络和算子理论，实现了对随机非线性动力系统的鲁棒建模与高效预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的随机非线性动力系统建模方法在处理高维复杂观测数据时往往面临可扩展性和非线性表征能力的瓶颈。现有的方法难以同时兼顾计算效率（如闭式解）和对复杂动力学行为的捕获能力。因此，研究者旨在开发一种结合深度学习的灵活性与算子理论（如Koopman算子）数学严谨性的新方法，以解决随机动力系统中的状态推断和预测问题。

Method: 本文提出了一种深度谱编码器（DSE），这是一种基于算子的潜状态空间模型。其核心方法包括：利用深度神经网络学习非线性特征映射，将观测映射为马尔可夫潜状态；利用函数型典型相关分析（Functional CCA）在可学习的Galerkin投影特征空间中构建状态坐标；利用脊回归（Ridge-regularized）的闭式解对转移算子和观测算子进行估计，并将其与协方差算子的Galerkin投影相结合。

Result: 实验结果表明，DSE模型在处理多个具有噪声和部分观测的复杂动态场景时，表现优于传统的序列贝叶斯滤波和动态模态分解基准方法。该模型展现了更高的稳定性和更强的预测准确性，验证了其在特征空间中进行序列贝叶斯滤波和Koopman谱模态分解的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的深度谱编码器（DSE）成功地将算子理论与深度学习相结合，为随机非线性动力系统提供了一种高效的潜状态空间建模框架。该方法通过闭式解优化算子，不仅提升了对复杂动态的表征能力，还增强了在噪声和部分观测环境下的鲁棒性，证明了算子学习在非线性系统分析中的巨大潜力。

Abstract: We propose a spectral learning method for stochastic nonlinear dynamical systems represented with embedded latent transfer operators in deep feature spaces. We instantiate the method as Deep Spectral Encoder (DSE), an operator-based latent state-space model in which a time-invariant neural encoder implements learnable nonlinear feature maps from observations, and these features define Markovian latent states whose temporal evolution and observation mapping are described by the transfer and observation operators, respectively. Functional canonical correlation analysis in a learnable Galerkin-projected feature space provides state coordinates from past and future observations, and the two linear operators are estimated on the state coordinates as ridge-regularized closed-form solutions that coincide with Galerkin projections of the associated covariance operators. On this representation, we generalize sequential Bayesian filtering and Koopman spectral mode decomposition in feature space. Experiments on several scenarios show stable and superior performance with sequential Bayesian filtering and dynamic mode decomposition baselines even under noise and partial observability.

</details>


### [113] [Lyapunov-Based Sample Complexity Analysis for Weakly-Coupled MDPs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14095)
*Tianhao Wu,Matthew Zurek,Weina Wang,Qiaomin Xie*

TL;DR: 本文研究了弱耦合马尔可夫决策过程（WCMDPs）和休止多臂老虎机（RBs）的样本复杂度，提出了一种基于Lyapunov函数的新型分析框架，成功证明了利用弱耦合结构可以将学习算法的复杂度降低至多项式级别。

Method: 本文采用基于生成模型的“即插即用”（Plug-in）方法，核心技术贡献在于提出了一种新型的基于Lyapunov的分析框架，并引入了漂移转移技术（drift transfer technique）以及针对线性规划松弛的细粒度扰动分析方法。

Result: 针对完全异构的WCMDP，首次建立了具有多项式复杂度和 $O(1/\sqrt{N})$ 优化间隙的有限样本PAC保证；对于同构的RBs，在温和的结构假设下实现了更小的优化间隙。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一套基于Lyapunov函数的分析框架，有效克服了传统偏差函数难以控制的难题，为弱耦合系统和线性规划（LP）松弛策略的分析提供了强有力的工具。研究结果表明，利用弱耦合结构，可以通过多项式复杂度的样本和计算成本实现近优策略。

Abstract: We study the sample complexity of learning in average-reward weakly-coupled Markov decision processes (WCMDPs) and Restless Bandits (RBs) under a generative model. Naive reduction to a tabular MDP leads to high complexity bounds as the state-action space is exponentially large in the number of arms $N$. By exploiting the weakly coupled structure, we show that near-optimal policies can be learned with sample and computational complexities that are polynomial in $N$. Specifically, we analyze the plug-in approach, which applies an efficient planning algorithm to an empirical model estimated from data. For fully heterogeneous WCMDPs, we establish the first finite-sample PAC guarantee with polynomial complexity and an $O(1/\sqrt{N})$ optimality gap. For homogeneous RBs, we further prove that a smaller optimality gap is achievable under mild structural assumptions. A primary technical contribution of our work is a novel Lyapunov-based analysis framework. Unlike classical approaches that rely on the difficult-to-control bias function, our framework uses an explicitly constructed Lyapunov function along with a drift transfer technique between the true and empirical models. A key step of independent interest in our framework is a fine-grained perturbation analysis for the underlying linear programming (LP) relaxation, which provides a general tool for analyzing LP-based policies and weakly-coupled systems.

*Suhyun Bae,Donghun Lee*

TL;DR: AOE 是一种无需训练的通用数字嵌入技术，通过结合实数值与 p-adic 特征来保留数学运算结构，成功解决了 AI 处理数字时的结构缺失问题，并在多项数学任务中展现了超越现有方法的卓越性能。
