Method: 提出了“阿德尔运算保持嵌入”（Adelic operation-preserved embeddings, AOE）。这是一种无需训练的表示方法，能够同时捕捉数字的实数值特性及其模（p-adic）特征，并通过设计保持加法和乘法结构，实现数值到数学化嵌入的转换。该方法具有即插即用的特性，可无缝集成到现有模型架构中。

Conclusion: AOE 为解决人工智能领域的“数字处理难题”提供了一条原则性的途径。通过在嵌入中融合算术与代数结构，该方法为模型处理数值任务提供了一个稳健、通用的基础，有望提升各类架构在数学推理任务上的表现。

Abstract: We introduce Adelic operation-preserved embeddings (AOE), a training-free representation that captures both a number's real value and its modular (p-adic) signatures. This construction preserves additive and multiplicative structure by design, turning numerical input into embeddings that "speak in the language of mathematics." Unlike prior approaches that rely on task-specific retraining, AOE is plug-and-play and drops seamlessly into existing architectures. On algebraic combinatorics benchmarks, it delivers consistent gains including the first-ever perfect accuracy on the Weaving Pattern task-while suggesting a principled path forward for overcoming the long-standing "number problem" in AI.

### [115] [DTVEM-RE: A Hierarchical Random-Effects Extension of the Differential Time-Varying Effect Model for Person-Specific Multi-Lag Estimation in Intensive Longitudinal Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14116)
*Amartya Bhattacharya*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 DTVEM-RE，这是对流行的时间变异效应模型 (DTVEM) 的扩展，首次允许在密集纵向数据分析中捕捉个体特异性的滞后效应，解决了原模型假设所有个体滞后结构一致的局限性，并在预测准确性和模型灵活性上均有显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原有的 DTVEM 模型假设所有个体共享相同的滞后结构，这与现代临床心理学研究中“个体间存在差异”的认知相悖，且原作者已将改进此局限性列为未来工作方向。此外，现有模型无法捕捉不同指标在不同滞后点上表现出的个体差异。

Method: 作者提出了 DTVEM-RE 模型，引入了个体特异性滞后系数。该方法包含两个版本：1) 基于 Stan 的离散时间分层贝叶斯向量自回归模型 (VAR)，用于跨个体汇集信息并提供校准后的不确定性估计；2) 基于 ctsem 的连续时间 Ornstein-Uhlenbeck 模型，专门用于处理观测时间点不均匀的情况。此外，作者还引入了多滞后版本以更全面地分析滞后结构。

Result: 1) 模拟测试显示贝叶斯版本能准确恢复个体间变异参数，偏差小于 0.01；2) 在真实数据集分析中，个体特异性滞后效应差异显著，DTVEM-RE 在单步预测中表现优于其他离散时间方法；3) 多滞后版本揭示了不同项目在不同滞后点上存在差异，这是传统 mlVAR 方法无法捕捉的；4) 贝叶斯与连续时间版本在估计结果上高度一致。

Conclusion: DTVEM-RE 是首个实现个体差异化滞后检测的 DTVEM 扩展模型，它克服了原模型假设所有个体具有相同滞后结构的局限性，更好地契合了现代临床研究中个体间存在差异的理念。该模型具有高度的灵活性和准确性，是处理密集纵向数据的有力工具。

Abstract: The Differential Time-Varying Effect Model (DTVEM) of Jacobson et al. (2019) is a popular tool for finding the best time lag in intensive longitudinal data, but it assumes everyone shares the same lag structure. The original authors named fixing this as future work, and it clashes with the premise of modern clinical research, which is that people differ. We present DTVEM-RE, an extension that lets each person have their own lag coefficients, with two versions of the confirmatory step: a discrete-time hierarchical Bayesian VAR in Stan, which pools across people and gives calibrated uncertainty, and a continuous-time per-person Ornstein-Uhlenbeck model in ctsem, which handles unevenly spaced beeps directly. We report four results. A simulation shows the Bayesian version recovers the between-person spread tau_a with bias below 0.01 and coverage of 90 to 93 percent. On the Fisher et al. (2017) EMA dataset (N=40), person-specific lag-1 effects vary by an order of magnitude across three mood items, the Bayesian and GAMM estimates agree closely (r=0.87 to 0.92), and DTVEM-RE gives the best one-step-ahead prediction among four discrete-time methods. A multi-lag version shows all nine tau_k values have credible intervals excluding zero, and the lag where people differ most changes across items, something lag-1-only methods like mlVAR cannot detect. Finally, the two versions agree almost exactly on person-specific lag-1 estimates (r >= 0.995), differing only as shrinkage predicts. DTVEM-RE is, to our knowledge, the first person-specific implementation of DTVEM-style lag detection, and it contains standard DTVEM as a special case.

</details>


### [116] [Recovering Stranded Discrimination in Knowledge Tracing: Per-Item Bias Correction via Empirical-Bayes Shrinkage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14123)
*Xiaoran Yan,Cheng Tang,Atsushi Shimada*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对固定部署的知识追踪模型存在的系统性偏差，该研究提出SLC（状态空间对数校正）方法，通过引入项目身份条件化处理，在提升概率校准的同时有效恢复了模型的判别性能（AUC），特别是在数据稀疏的项目上效果显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 知识追踪模型部署后通常保持固定，但在实际应用中会因主干架构的表达能力限制及部署后的环境变化产生系统性的“项目对数偏差”（per-item logit bias），导致预测性能下降。传统的全局校准方法（如Platt缩放）虽能提升概率校准度，但无法改善模型的判别能力（AUC），作者旨在解决这一局限性。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为SLC（State-space Logit Correction）的方法。该方法首先将二元观测值通过Laplace/IRLS转换为高斯伪观测值，利用卡尔曼平滑器执行经验贝叶斯收缩，并拟合偏移-Platt链接函数。其核心在于通过状态空间建模，在校准概率的同时，基于项目身份信息恢复模型的判别能力。

Result: 在四个数据集、五个主干架构及三个随机种子的实验中，SLC在所有数据集上均提升了AUC，并在三个数据集上改善了负对数似然（NLL），且这种性能优势在稀疏样本（sparse items）上表现尤为明显。研究还通过实验证明了该现象在教育领域之外也具有普适性。

Conclusion: SLC方法有效地解决了知识追踪模型在部署后出现的系统性偏差问题。通过引入针对项目身份的校正机制，该研究证明了在保持模型主干不变的情况下，依然可以通过条件化校正提升判别能力（AUC）和概率估计质量。此外，研究提出的可检测性界限为理解模型性能上限提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Deployed knowledge-tracing models are typically frozen after training, yet systematic per-item logit bias arises, from limited per-item expressivity in backbone architectures and from post-deployment shifts in item properties, degrading prediction quality. Global post-hoc calibrators such as Platt scaling, temperature scaling, and isotonic regression improve probability estimates but leave discriminative ability, as measured by AUC, unchanged. This AUC invariance is a structural consequence of monotone score-only transforms; recovering the stranded discrimination requires conditioning on item identity. We propose SLC (State-space Logit Correction), which converts binary observations to Gaussian pseudo-observations via Laplace/IRLS, applies empirical-Bayes shrinkage through a Kalman smoother, and fits an offset-Platt link. The state-space formulation also yields a detectability bound that characterizes the Bernoulli information floor, explaining why temporal tracking provides no benefit at current data densities. Across four datasets, five backbones, and three seeds, SLC improves AUC on all four datasets and NLL on three, with the advantage concentrating on sparse items. Cross-domain controls suggest that the same phenomenon can arise beyond education when the deployed backbone leaves entity-level bias.

### [117] [Contract-Based Compositional Shielding for Safe Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14130)
*Omar Adalat,Edwin Hamel-De le Court,Francesco Belardinelli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多智能体安全协作框架，通过将全局安全目标转化为相互依赖的局部契约，在无需中心化运行时控制的情况下，实现了多智能体系统在复杂环境下的安全与性能优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多智能体强化学习中，单一智能体往往无法通过自身行为强制执行全局安全，而简单的去中心化防护机制（shields）又常因过度保守而排除掉需要协作才能实现的最优安全策略。因此，研究旨在寻找一种既能保持去中心化执行，又能通过协作达成全局安全规范的方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于线性时序逻辑（LTL_safe）的契约式协作方法。主要步骤包括：1. 将全局安全规范分解为多个智能体的局部义务组合；2. 利用契约机制，确保一组局部义务的合取逻辑上隐含全局安全要求；3. 在训练期间，通过非平稳多臂老虎机（non-stationary multi-armed bandit）从预定义的义务库中动态选择最优义务组合，从而优化团队奖励并保持安全性。

Result: 在6个不同的环境和15种算法变体中的实验表明，该方法能够有效地在复杂的协同任务中实现端到端的安全性保障，同时显著优于传统的去中心化防护方法，成功在安全性和团队奖励之间取得了平衡。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种名为“契约式协作”（contractual coordination）的新型多智能体强化学习框架，证明了通过将全局安全性分解为相互关联的局部义务，可以在不牺牲去中心化执行的前提下，实现最优且安全的多智能体协作。该方法成功克服了传统去中心化防护机制无法处理协作性安全问题的局限性。

Abstract: Safe coordination problems surface in multi-agent reinforcement learning when global safety cannot be enforced by any agent unilaterally: the admissibility of one agent's action may depend on the dynamics of other agents. Decentralised shields can enforce safety at runtime, but purely factorised permissions often exclude optimal team behaviour that is safe only through coordination. We study deterministic safety guarantees for agents trained and deployed under decentralised execution, recovering team-optimal safe behaviour without centralised runtime control. Agents have a shared global specification $φ$ in the safety fragment of Linear Temporal Logic ($\mathsf{LTL}_{\mathsf{safe}}$ ), and select among tuples of local $\mathsf{LTL}_{\mathsf{safe}}$ obligations whose conjunction implies the global specification $φ$. Each agent may rely on the other agents' local obligations as assumptions because the whole contract tuple is certified simultaneously and allows projection into local action masks. At learning time, a non-stationary multi-armed bandit chooses among a library of local $\mathsf{LTL}_{\mathsf{safe}}$ obligations to select the tuple that optimises team reward, all without forgoing end-to-end safety. We evaluate the approach across 6 environments and 15 algorithmic variants.

### [118] [Decoupled Latent Optimization of Diffusion Models for Full Waveform Inversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14139)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了“解耦潜在优化”（Decoupled Latent Optimization, DLO）方法。该方法将标准的潜在优化公式放宽为针对辅助物理变量和潜在变量的二次惩罚目标函数，使得数据保真度梯度在物理空间直接作用，而扩散模型采样仅通过解码后的先验样本贡献，同时保留了传统FWI的平滑速度初始化策略。

Result: 在OpenFWI基准测试中，DLO在干净、噪声及缺迹数据条件下均优于传统正则化方法和现有的扩散模型方法。此外，在Marmousi和Overthrust数据集上的测试表明，DLO能有效恢复复杂的断层结构，且对初始化平滑程度和测量噪声具有稳健性。

Abstract: Full waveform inversion (FWI) recovers subsurface velocity from seismic recordings by solving a severely ill-posed, nonconvex PDE-constrained optimization. Classical regularizers stabilize the inversion but fail to reproduce realistic geological structures; recent diffusion-prior methods improve realism at the cost of a fragile trade-off between data fidelity and prior consistency. We propose Decoupled Latent Optimization (DLO), which relaxes the standard latent-optimization formulation into a quadratic-penalty objective over an auxiliary physical variable and a latent variable. The data-fidelity gradient acts in physical space, the diffusion sampler contributes only through a decoded prior sample, and the standard smoothed-velocity initialization of classical FWI is preserved. On the OpenFWI benchmark, DLO outperforms classical regularizers and existing diffusion-based methods under clean, noisy, and missing-trace acquisitions. The prior, trained on 70*70 OpenFWI models, transfers directly to the Marmousi and Overthrust benchmarks, where DLO recovers intricate fault structures and remains robust to initialization smoothing and measurement noise.

### [119] [Trust but Verify: Mitigating Medical Hallucinations via Post-Hoc Adversarial Auditing and Multi-Agent Feedback Loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14149)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究团队构建了一个基于单一LLM骨干的五智能体“信任但验证（Trust but Verify）”系统。通过创建一个包含103个临床多项选择题的对抗性数据集（涉及已被禁用或撤市的药物）来评估模型性能，并对比了GPT-OSS、Llama-3、Falcon-3等模型在原始模式与智能体模式下的表现。

This study examine whether LLMs recommend recently banned or withdrawn pharmaceuticals when answering clinical questions and tests an agent-based method for reducing such errors. We developed a five-agent "Trust but Verify" system using a single LLM backbone. To measure regulatory knowledge obsolescence, we created an adversarial dataset of 103 clinical MCQs where historically correct answers now refer to banned substances. This scale ensures statistical significance across various therapeutic classes. We evaluated three open-access model families (GPT-OSS, Llama-3, Falcon-3) under vanilla and agentic conditions. Performance was measured via pointwise score, label accuracy, Hallucination Error Rate (HER), and Component Fidelity (CF) score. We also observed clinical safety regression in proprietary models. In default configurations, all models showed high hallucination rates, consistently selecting banned drugs that matched training data patterns. Our proposed agentic architecture reduced HER by approximately 53% across models. Pointwise scores shifted from -0.25 (unsafe recommendation) toward 0.0 (appropriate refusal). The safety audit intercepted dangerous outputs even when models' parametric knowledge favored the banned substance. The proposed multi-agent framework offers a model-agnostic method for enforcing regulatory compliance that prioritizes patient safety over fluent text generation. Our work demonstrates a practical approach for deploying autonomous AI systems in safety-critical healthcare settings. It shows how real-time regulatory data can be integrated into LLM pipelines to support clinical decision-making.

</details>


### [120] [Small LLMs: Pruning vs. Training from Scratch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14150)
*Yufeng Xu,Taiming Lu,Kunjun Li,Jiachen Zhu,Mingjie Sun,Zhuang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文评估了Llama-3.1-8B在不同剪枝粒度和训练预算下的表现，发现剪枝在受限资源下具有明显优势，但当训练资源充足时，粗粒度剪枝的优势会消失，此时从零训练可能更具竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究剪枝技术是否真正能够成为构建高效、轻量级语言模型的捷径，以及在不同训练预算和剪枝粒度下，预训练父模型所带来的知识传递优势是否依然稳健。

Method: 研究人员对Llama-3.1-8B模型进行剪枝（剪枝比率0.5-0.8），涵盖深度、宽度和稀疏性三种粒度的六种方法，并在两种受控的Token匹配设置下评估模型性能：一是固定训练Token预算，对比剪枝初始化与随机初始化；二是固定总计算预算，对比剪枝与从零开始训练。

Result: 1. 在相同Token预算下，剪枝初始化优于随机初始化，但该优势随Token预算增加和剪枝率升高而减弱；2. 在总训练预算一致的前提下，细粒度剪枝仍保留优势，但粗粒度结构化剪枝的优势可被从零训练所超越，表明预训练带来的知识传递主要体现在细粒度层面。

Conclusion: 当拥有大型预训练模型且训练数据受限时，剪枝优于从零开始训练；但在训练资源充足的情况下，针对较粗粒度的剪枝方法，从零开始训练可以达到或超过剪枝的效果，这意味着大型预训练模型并非在所有场景下都是必需的。

Abstract: Pruning promises a shortcut to strong small language models. In this work, we examine this promise by pruning Llama-3.1-8B at pruning ratios of 0.5--0.8 with six methods spanning depth, width, and sparse granularities, under two controlled token-matched settings. (1) With the same training token budget, pruned initialization consistently outperforms random initialization. This shows that the parent model provides a strong starting point, although the advantage narrows as the training token budget grows and as the pruning ratio rises, nearly vanishing at the highest pruning ratio we study. (2) When training from scratch is instead given the full token budget consumed by the whole pipeline, pruning at finer granularities still retains an advantage, while coarser structured pruning can be matched or surpassed. This suggests that the parent model transfers knowledge that additional training tokens alone cannot fully recover, but only at fine granularity. Taken together, our results yield a clear recommendation: with a large pretrained model in hand and a limited training token budget, pruning is better than training from scratch; when the training budget is not limited, training from scratch can be competitive for coarser pruning, so a large pretrained parent is not always necessary.

</details>


### [121] [Graph-based Target Back-Propagation for Context Adaptation in Multi-LLM Agentic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14155)
*Tan Zhu,Tong Yao,Kananart Kuwaranancharoen,Amit Singh,Yushang Lai,Deepa Mohan,Shankara Bhargava*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为“基于图的目标反向传播”（GTBP）框架。该方法将智能体工作流建模为有向无环图（DAG），通过将局部目标输出沿着图反向传播，利用目标与实际输出之间的差异来指导各阶段提示词的迭代更新，从而实现无需微调模型权重即可完成系统级优化。

Result: 实验结果表明，GTBP在三个基准测试中均显著优于现有的强基线模型，且在保持计算成本可控的前提下，实现了更优的性能表现。此外，理论分析也验证了该方法的稳定性及降低整体优化目标的能力。

Conclusion: GTBP通过图反向传播机制成功解决了多智能体系统中提示词自动优化的难题，既在理论上证明了收敛性，又在实验中展现了优于现有方法的性能，为构建高效、可自适应的智能体工作流提供了重要的技术参考。

Abstract: Context adaptation automates prompt engineering in LLM-based systems by iteratively revising tunable prompts from task feedback, without modifying model weights. Extending this paradigm to multi-LLM agentic systems is crucial: existing methods suffer from inaccurate credit assignment and lack convergence guarantees. We propose \textbf{G}raph-based \textbf{T}arget \textbf{B}ack-\textbf{P}ropagation (GTBP), a context adaptation framework for agentic workflows modeled as directed acyclic graphs. GTBP propagates local target outputs backward through the workflow graph and uses target--output discrepancies to guide a stage-wise prompt update mechanism. Theoretically, we show that GTBP's stage-wise prompt updates become stable over iterations, and that a sufficiently capable LLM optimizer can decrease the overall objective. Empirically, GTBP consistently outperforms strong baselines across three benchmarks while maintaining comparable computational cost.

Method: 提出了一种名为CDPR的方法，利用子模最大化（submodular maximization）技术构建规则集。通过设计两种基于该理论的算法，在保证规则集判别能力和简约性的同时，提供了覆盖率方面的理论保证。

Abstract: Learning systems based on IF-THEN rule representations readily offer interpretability, making them a crucial focus in contemporary AI research. While existing state-of-the-art algorithms implicitly prioritize predictive accuracy, they often fall short on one or more quality metrics that ensure interpretability, such as coverage and parsimony of rule sets. Motivated by this, this paper propose the development of CDPR, which aims to create highly accurate and interpretable rule sets for classification problems. To the best of our knowledge, this represents the first attempt to establish such an approach. In this study, we introduce two algorithms rooted in submodular maximization, which not only provide provable guarantees on coverage but also yield rule sets that are both discriminative and parsimonious. ### [123] [Learning Urban Access Costs from Origin-Destination Flows via Inverse Optimal Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14157)
*Paula Joy B. Martinez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究利用最优传输理论和机器学习方法，通过分析学校间的入学流动数据，量化了家庭在公共服务选择中的隐性成本，并成功评估了政府补贴对减轻出行成本的实际效果，为城市公共服务的空间优化提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用逆向最优传输（Inverse Optimal Transport）框架，将学校间的入学流动视为熵正则化的最优传输方案。具体包括两种模型：一是具有补贴项的“距离区间模型”（ interpretable distance-banded model）；二是基于“可微Sinkhorn正向传递”（differentiable Sinkhorn forward pass）训练的神经网络成本模型。通过这些模型，作者量化了补贴对家庭出行成本的抵消效应。

Result: 通过对菲律宾人口最稠密地区约28万次学生出行的分析，研究成功估算出补贴等效距离（λ），即补贴在家庭感知中抵消了多少公里的出行成本。结果显示该框架能将宏观行政数据转化为具有可解释性的规划指标。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用行政性起点-终点（O-D）数据，结合逆向最优传输模型，能够有效量化城市服务中的隐性成本，从而为政府在补贴设计、公共设施选址及资源优化配置方面提供科学的决策支持。

Abstract: Cities deliver basic services through mixed public-private facility networks, including schools, clinics, transit providers, and subsidized service points. In these systems, planners often observe where households go, but not the latent cost function through which they trade off factors such as distance, price, and institutional access. We study this urban problem through school choice in the Philippines, where the country's largest national education subsidy is intended to redirect learners from congested public schools to participating private schools. Treating school-to-school enrollment flows as an entropic optimal transport plan, we recover latent choice costs using two complementary inverse optimal transport models: an interpretable distance-banded model with a subsidy term, and a neural cost model trained through a differentiable Sinkhorn forward pass. Applied to 283{,}016 learner trips across 23{,}820 observed flows in the most populated region, the framework estimates a subsidy-equivalent distance, $λ^{(k)}$, interpreted as the kilometers of perceived travel cost offset by the subsidy. The case demonstrates how administrative origin-destination data can be transformed into interpretable planning metrics for accessibility-aware subsidy design, facility siting, and urban service allocation.

### [124] [Curvature-Guided Geometric Representation for Protein-Ligand Binding Affinity Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14159)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Protein-ligand binding affinity (PLA) prediction is critical in drug discovery. Despite the notable advancements in machine learning-based approaches, existing methods struggle to jointly characterize local geometric organization and globally coordinated cross-molecular interactions, limiting their ability to model complex binding mechanisms. Here, we propose RicciBind, a geometric representation framework that integrates curvature-guided hierarchical structure learning with optimal transport (OT)-based cross-domain alignment to model molecular interactions. Specifically, RicciBind leverages Ricci curvature to capture local interaction tightness within molecular structures, enhancing structural awareness and organizing atomic interactions into curvature-aware hierarchical representations. An OT-based cluster matching mechanism then aligns protein and ligand clusters across heterogeneous domains under geometric constraints, enabling globally consistent correspondences and revealing higher-order interaction patterns beyond local neighborhoods. By coupling curvature-guided structure encoding with OT-driven cross-domain alignment, RicciBind effectively models complex interaction semantics and substantially improves both the accuracy and interpretability of binding affinity prediction. Extensive experiments demonstrate that RicciBind achieved superior predictive performance and generalization across PLA benchmarks and virtual screening tasks. Ablation studies further confirmed the essential role of Ricci curvature in enhancing molecular interaction representations.

### [126] [Context-aware Modality-Topology Co-Alignment for Multimodal Attributed Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14172)
*Sirui Zhang,Xu Wang,Zhengyu Wu,Xunkai Li,Hongchao Qin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CoMAG 是一种新型的多模态属性图骨干网络，通过任务自适应的图上下文学习和模态保留的对齐策略，解决了多模态图表示学习中信息丢失和任务适配性差的问题，实现了在多种复杂任务上的卓越表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MAG方法过度依赖固定的图结构或采用统一的特征融合，导致在处理需要精细模态对应关系的跨模态任务时，无法根据不同任务需求动态调整传播机制，且由于过度压缩导致模态特定信息的丢失。

Method: 1. 可靠上下文学习（Reliable Context Learning）：基于多模态语义一致性评估边可靠性，并通过任务感知门控机制选择上下文组件，补充原始拓扑结构。
2. 模态保留跳跃令牌对齐（Modality-preserving Hop-token Alignment）：维护模态特定的多跳轨迹，通过跨模态匹配令牌并解耦共享与私有表示，从而在保留模态特异性信息的同时实现对齐。

Conclusion: CoMAG 提供了一种高效且通用的多模态属性图（MAG）骨干网络。通过学习任务自适应的可靠上下文和模态保留对齐，该方法有效解决了传统模型中任务不可知传播和特征过压缩的问题，在图级预测、跨模态匹配和图条件生成任务中均展现出优越性能，并保持了线性的计算复杂度。

Abstract: Multimodal Attributed Graphs (MAGs) model real-world entities by coupling graph topology with heterogeneous attributes such as text and images. They support graph-centric tasks requiring structural and class-discriminative representations, and modality-centric tasks requiring fine-grained cross-modal correspondence. However, existing MAG methods often rely on fixed graph contexts or uniformly fused representations, causing task-agnostic propagation and over-compressed fusion that hinder diverse task requirements and modality-specific evidence preservation. To address this, we propose CoMAG, a unified MAG backbone that learns task-adaptive reliable contexts and modality-preserving alignment within them. CoMAG first conducts Reliable Context Learning by estimating edge reliability from multimodal semantic consistency, complementing raw topology with semantic neighbors, and selecting context components through a task-aware gate. It then performs Modality-preserving Hop-token Alignment by maintaining modality-specific multi-hop trajectories, matching modality-hop tokens across modalities, and decoupling shared and private representations. Thus, CoMAG produces graph and modality representations from one forward pass while retaining modality-specific cues. We further analyze stable propagation, over-smoothing mitigation, and modality-collapse control. Experiments on nine OpenMAG datasets compare CoMAG with feature-only, graph-only, multimodal, and unified MAG baselines across graph-level prediction, modality matching, and graph-conditioned generation. Results show that CoMAG achieves the best reported performance, demonstrating that task-adaptive reliable contexts and modality-preserving alignment improve structural prediction, cross-modal matching, and graph-conditioned generation while retaining sparse edge-linear complexity.

### [127] [Zeta: Dual Whitening for Matrix Optimization via Coordinate-Adaptive Preconditioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14187)
*Kaiwen Chen,Shuhai Zhang,Qiuwu Chen,Zimo Liu,Linxiao Li,Ying Sun,Yuchen Li,Yifan Zhang,Bo Han,Mingkui Tan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对矩阵感知优化器在处理尺度异构性时的脆弱性，本文提出了Zeta优化器。它通过先进行坐标白化以纠正尺度不平衡，再进行谱白化，从而显著提升了神经网络训练的稳定性、收敛速度和最终泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有如Muon等矩阵感知优化器严重依赖Newton-Schulz迭代，而该迭代过程极易受到输入矩阵中坐标维度尺度不平衡（异构性）的影响，导致训练不稳定或收敛缓慢。因此，需要一种能够先行处理尺度偏差的机制。

Method: 1. 揭示问题：通过卡方一致性检验验证了动量矩阵中普遍存在的坐标尺度异构性（Scale Heterogeneity）。2. 算法设计：提出Zeta优化器，构建了“坐标白化 -> 谱白化”的严格有序流水线。3. 理论分析：从数学上证明该双重流程通过改善输入条件数，能显著降低正交化误差。

Result: 在0.6B到8B参数规模的语言模型、混合专家（MoE）架构及视觉任务中，Zeta均能匹配或超越主流基线模型，证明了在正交化前消除尺度不平衡对于加速收敛和提升泛化能力具有关键作用。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Zeta优化器通过先进行坐标白化再进行谱白化的双重白化流程，有效解决了矩阵感知优化器中输入规模异构性带来的性能限制，为大规模神经网络训练提供了一种更稳健、更高效的优化方案。

Abstract: Large-scale neural network training increasingly relies on matrix-aware optimizers that exploit the structure of weight parameters beyond element-wise adaptation. However, existing matrix-aware methods such as Muon have an underappreciated vulnerability: their core operation, Newton-Schulz iteration, depends critically on input conditioning, yet the raw momentum matrices exhibit severe coordinate-wise scale heterogeneity. In this paper, we first verify this scale heterogeneity through a chi-square uniformity test, showing that intra-matrix scale imbalance is prevalent across Transformer layers and that coordinate whitening effectively corrects it. Motivated by this finding, we propose Zeta, a dual whitening optimizer that applies coordinate whitening and spectral whitening in a strictly ordered pipeline. The ordering is not a tunable choice but follows from a mathematical dependency: coordinate whitening establishes the statistical isotropy that spectral whitening requires to function reliably. We further prove that this dual pipeline strictly reduces orthogonalization error relative to pure spectral methods by improving the condition number of the input. Empirically, Zeta matches or surpasses strong baselines across language modeling (0.6B to 8B parameters), mixture-of-experts architectures, and vision tasks, demonstrating that resolving scale imbalance before orthogonalization leads to faster convergence and better generalization. Code is available at https://gitcode.com/kevin259/MindSpeed.

</details>


### [128] [Simplex-Constrained Sparse Bagging: Transitioning from Uniform Priors to Sparse Posteriors in Ensemble Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13589)
*Meher Sai Preetam,Meher Bhaskar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SCSB提出了一种新型Bagging集成优化框架，通过引入凹二次惩罚项在单纯形上实现权重稀疏化，在大幅压缩模型规模、加速推理的同时，显著改善了预测的概率校准效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Bagging集成方法（如随机森林）对所有基估计器赋予相等的投票权重，忽略了不同基估计器在局部表现上的差异，且容易导致模型预测过自信。此外，集成模型庞大的规模限制了其在资源受限场景下的推理速度。

Method: 该研究提出了“单纯形约束稀疏装袋（SCSB）”框架，将集成剪枝与概率校准建模为单纯形上的联合优化问题。为解决L1范数在单纯形上恒定导致的剪枝失效（L1-单纯形悖论），引入了凹二次惩罚项以诱导权重稀疏化，并利用袋外（OOB）损失进行优化。

Result: SCSB实现了高达96%的集成模型压缩率，显著提升了推理速度，降低了预期校准误差（ECE），并在多数情况下维持或提升了原始模型的泛化准确率。

Conclusion: SCSB通过数学上严谨的联合优化框架，有效解决了传统Bagging集成模型冗余、推理速度慢及预测过自信的问题。该方法证明了在保持或提升泛化精度的同时，实现高效模型压缩与校准的可行性。

Abstract: We present Simplex-Constrained Sparse Bagging (SCSB), a mathematically rigorous framework for post-training compression and probability calibration of bootstrap-based bagging ensembles. Standard bagging ensembles (such as Random Forests, Bagged SVMs, and Bagged Neural Networks) assign uniform voting power to all constituent estimators. However, this naive uniform prior ignores the varying local competence of base estimators and contributes to model overconfidence. We formulate ensemble pruning and calibration as a joint optimization problem over the probability simplex by minimizing the Out-Of-Bag (OOB) loss. To induce sparsity, we address the theoretical "L1-simplex paradox" -- the mathematical reality that the L1 norm is constant on the simplex and fails to prune -- by introducing a concave quadratic penalty. SCSB is model-agnostic and achieves up to 96% ensemble compression, yielding linear inference speedups and superior probability calibration (lowered Expected Calibration Error) while preserving or enhancing generalization accuracy.

To mitigate these limitations, we propose DRIVE (Distributional and Retrieval-Augmented Bidding with Value Evaluation), a unified Transformer-based framework that decouples candidate action generation from decision making for offline auto-bidding.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为CPES的图神经网络模型。该方法首先利用势能曲面的Hessian矩阵推导出曲率谱描述符，以表征构象柔性；其次，通过谱交叉注意力机制对比结合前后的动态变化；同时，利用几何感知消息传递和软聚类等技术学习静态结构特征；最后，将动态曲率信息与静态结构交互表征融合，进行亲和力回归预测。

Conclusion: 本研究通过将基于几何的深度学习与物理驱动的势能曲面曲率特征相结合，证明了显式建模分子构象柔性对于提升亲和力预测精度的重要性，为药物发现提供了更具物理可解释性的计算工具。

Abstract: Accurate prediction of protein-ligand binding affinity is essential for structure-based drug discovery. Recent geometric deep learning methods have achieved promising performance by representing protein-ligand complexes as three-dimensional graphs. However, most existing approaches mainly rely on static interaction geometry from a single bound conformation, while neglecting molecular flexibility and binding-induced conformational changes. To address this limitation, we propose a curvature-informed potential energy surface (CPES) graph neural network for protein-ligand binding affinity prediction, which incorporates physics-informed curvature representations to model conformational flexibility. CPES first derives curvature spectral descriptors from the Hessian of the potential energy surface evaluated at equilibrium configurations, whose eigenvalues define the local principal curvatures of the potential energy surface. It then uses spectral cross-attention to compare the unbound ligand and protein with the bound complex, thereby capturing binding-induced changes in conformational dynamics. In parallel, hierarchical protein-ligand interaction representations are learned from static structural features through geometry-aware message passing, soft clustering, and bidirectional cross-attention. Finally, CPES fuses the curvature-informed dynamic representations with static interaction representations for affinity regression. Extensive evaluations on multiple benchmark datasets demonstrate that CPES achieves improved predictive performance and offers physical interpretability.

### [133] [Learning the Context of Errors: Black-Box Online Adaptation of Time Series Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14222)

Method: 作者提出了名为“在线残差上下文适配”（ORCA）的方法。该方法的核心在于通过学习预测误差与“输入-输出上下文”之间的映射关系来修正基模型的预测结果，而无需进行参数微调或梯度反向传播，从而适应了黑盒API的限制。

Abstract: The rapid evolution of Time Series Foundation Models (TSFMs) has advanced zero-shot forecasting across diverse domains. This paradigm mismatch raises a question: In black-box online adaptation for TSFMs, what should we learn? We answer this with an insight: the predictive errors of the base model are conditioned on both the input and output of the base model (i.e., the context of errors). To validate this insight, we propose ORCA (Online Residual Contextual Adaptation). We conduct extensive experiments across 5 state-of-the-art TSFMs and 8 datasets to demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach. Abstract: Variational Inference (VI) is a fundamental inference technique in Bayesian machine learning for approximating complex posterior distributions. Recent advancements have leveraged neural networks to model implicit distributions, offering increased flexibility. We present an interpretability audit of BridgeDPI architecture on three different datasets including Gao, Human, and C.elegans. This study combines gradient-based attributions -- integrated gradients, saliency, layer-wise relevance propagation, SmoothGrad, and SmoothGrad-IG -- with feature-wise occlusion ablation and strict intersection consensus across methods to reduce single-explainer bias. We summarize sensitivity and signed effects at raw inputs, at the bridge similarity scaffold, and through the graph convolution, including edge-level sensitivities and targeted edge removals. The results show that explainability is most informative when treated as model criticism: it reveals modality dominance, padding and special-token artifacts, dataset-dependent cooperative versus suppressive effects across layers, and chemistry-consistent fragment and composition motifs where methods agree. These analyses do not substitute for structural or experimental ground truth, yet they can provide testable hypotheses for downstream validation in computational drug discovery pipelines. More broadly, applying modern XAI to contemporary DTI/DTA models is still an early pass over the rich structure implicit in trained weights and data -- yet even this first layer of scrutiny already helps researchers relate predictions to drug- and target-side representations and to prioritize external validation.

</details>


### [136] [Beyond a Single Explanation of the Adam--SGD Gap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14259)
*Chenxiang Zhang,Rustem Islamov,Enea Monzio Compagnoni,Jun Pang,Aurelien Lucchi,Antonio Orvieto*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过广泛的实证研究发现，Adam与SGD的性能差距源于数据和架构的复杂交互，而非单一因素。研究提出了“交叉批次大小”这一关键概念，解释了为何优化器优势会随批次大小变化，从而统一了此前零散的理论假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对Adam与SGD性能差距原因的探讨通常是孤立的，导致不同因素的相对重要性不明。本文旨在通过综合性的实证分析，重新审视这些假设，以揭示导致优化器性能差异的本质原因，并试图调和现有文献中相互冲突的观点。

Method: 作者通过跨视觉、语言、基因组学和图神经网络等多种任务，结合现代与经典架构进行受控的实证研究。通过系统性地评估数据分布（如词汇分布）、架构调整（如ReLU与GeLU的对比）及批次大小等因素，建立了一个理论上的性能差距模型来解释观察到的现象。

Result: 实证结果表明，没有单一因素能稳定解释Adam-SGD的性能差距。差距的大小表现出高度的背景依赖性，受数据分布特征和模型架构细节的显著影响。研究关键发现是一个通用的“交叉批次大小”现象：随着批次大小的增加，优化器的性能优势会在Adam和SGD之间发生转移，这一模型准确预测了实验中的趋势。

Conclusion: Adam与SGD之间的性能差距并非由单一因素造成，而是数据特征与模型架构之间复杂交互的结果。研究发现存在一个“交叉批次大小（crossover batch size）”，在该临界点，优化器的性能优势会发生反转，这一规律能够有效整合现有的各种解释，并为跨领域的超参数选择提供理论指导。

Abstract: Prior work has identified several factors that can contribute to the performance gap between Adam and SGD, spanning data aspects, architecture design, and optimization properties. Yet these explanations are often studied in isolation, leaving their relative importance unclear. In this work, we revisit these hypotheses through a controlled empirical study across vision, language, genomics, and graph tasks, spanning modern and classical architectures, and carefully designed training setups. Our results suggest that no single factor consistently explains the Adam--SGD gap. For instance, the Adam advantage can (1) persist under a uniform vocabulary distribution yet nearly disappear under a heavy-tailed one; (2) reverse in favor of SGD in softmax-attention models; and (3) become larger under soft architectural modifications, e.g., when ReLU is replaced by a GeLU nonlinearity. This suggests that the gap arises from nontrivial data and architecture interactions, rather than from a single common factor. Yet, we observe a pattern across our settings: a \emph{crossover batch size} at which the relative advantage shifts from SGD to Adam as the batch size scales. These empirical results are captured by our theoretical gap model, which predicts this batch-size-dependent crossover. Our perspective helps reconcile several existing hypotheses while offering practical insights across domains.

### [137] [DIFF-ERO: A Conformance-Aware Loss for Deep Learning in Process Mining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14283)
*Johannes De Smedt,Jari Peeperkorn,Artem Polyvyanyy,Jochen De Weerdt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 DIFF-ERO 的新型损失函数，旨在解决深度学习在流程挖掘中无法有效捕捉全局控制流结构的难题。通过将一致性评估可微分化并引入反向传播，该方法显著提升了预测模型的结构准确性和对流程模型的还原能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习在流程挖掘中的应用虽广，但标准的交叉熵损失函数仅关注局部下一步的预测准确性，难以显式捕捉流程的整体控制流结构。这导致模型在局部指标良好时，往往表现出不符合流程逻辑的全局行为（即缺乏一致性）。因此，研究者旨在开发一种能直接将控制流结构纳入训练目标的损失函数，以提升模型对复杂业务流程的建模能力。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为 DIFF-ERO 的一致性感知损失函数。其核心是将基于熵的随机一致性（Stochastic Conformance）转化为可微分的形式。具体而言，该方法通过在训练批次中构建具有软边成员资格的随机转移矩阵，将结构性的精确率（Precision）和召回率（Recall）作为反馈信号直接参与反向传播。它与模型结构无关，可与交叉熵损失函数联合使用。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，使用 DIFF-ERO 的模型在强调结构特征的预测任务中表现优于传统方法，同时在其他指标上保持竞争力。实验结果表明，模型学习到的随机自动机能够显著收敛于真实的过程结构，证明了模型成功内化了过程逻辑。

Conclusion: DIFF-ERO 成功地将过程挖掘中的一致性要求融入到了深度学习的训练目标中。该方法不仅提升了预测性能，还增强了模型内部对过程逻辑结构的理解，证明了在过程分析任务中，显式地将结构一致性约束加入损失函数是提升模型全局表现的有效手段。

Abstract: Deep learning has driven many recent advances in process analytics, especially for predictive and prescriptive monitoring. However, standard objectives such as cross-entropy optimize local next-step likelihoods and only implicitly capture control-flow structure. As a result, models can achieve high token-level accuracy while permitting imprecise global behaviour. We introduce DIFF-ERO, a conformance-aware loss function for deep learning models on process data. DIFF-ERO is a differentiable formulation of entropy-based stochastic conformance that incorporates control-flow information during training. Our approach constructs batch-level stochastic transition matrices with soft edge memberships, allowing structural precision and recall signals to directly inform backpropagation. The loss is model-agnostic and can be applied whenever the final representation parametrizes stochastic transitions. We instantiate DIFF-ERO in transformer encoder-decoder pipelines for next-activity prediction and use it jointly with cross-entropy to analyse its theoretical components with respect to convergence. Across benchmarks comparing other loss functions and targets, DIFF-ERO shows improved predictive performance where structure matters most while maintaining parity elsewhere. At the same time, the learned stochastic automaton converges towards the structural ground truth, indicating that the network internalizes process model structure.

To address these limitations, we propose a hierarchical ordinary differential equation clustering network, which utilizes neural ordinary differential equation to model latent state evolution as a continuous integral curve. This formulation enforces temporal continuity to effectively disentangle smooth feature trends from stochastic noise, while our adaptive hierarchical mechanism autonomously determines the appropriate number of prototypes without rigid prior constraints. Validated on the early link failure detection task with irregularly sampled time series, the proposed method effectively extracts underlying physical prototypes, thereby enabling robust failure detection. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多领域大模型训练中，单一模型的微调或单向蒸馏往往导致灾难性遗忘或知识偏见。研究动机在于探索如何让两个在不同领域各具优势的模型通过协作互教，实现双赢的“帕累托改进”。

Method: 提出了“在线策略协同蒸馏”（OPCoD）方法。其核心机制包括：1. 基于自身正确路径与同伴反馈的双重条件蒸馏；2. 认知门控（Cognizance-based gating）决定反馈时机；3. 反馈锚定（Feedback anchoring）将反馈落实于具体问题，从而实现高效的跨领域知识交换。

Result: 在Science Q&A任务上，OPCoD方法在所有被评估的领域对和学生模型中均表现优于基线模型，成功实现了跨领域的帕累托改进。

Conclusion: 研究证明，通过On-Policy Co-Distillation (OPCoD) 机制，多领域大模型可以通过相互协作实现帕累托改进，在提升跨领域表现的同时保持原有领域的优势，为多智能体协同进化提供了一种高效的范式。

Abstract: We study multi-domain LLM training in which two models, each stronger in a different domain, co-evolve by tutoring each other through on-policy feedback. Unlike one-way distillation or single-model fine-tuning, our goal is mutual Pareto improvement: each model improves across domains without losing its original strength. To this end, we propose On-Policy Co-Distillation (OPCoD), where each student's self-distillation is conditioned on its own correct rollout and feedback from its peer. To make feedback exchange effective, OPCoD uses cognizance-based gating to decide when to give feedback and feedback anchoring to ground feedback in the problem. On Science Q\&A tasks, OPCoD consistently outperforms baselines and achieves Pareto improvement across all evaluated domain pairs and students.

### [140] [Riemannian Metric Matching for Scalable Geometric Modeling of Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14334)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于去噪概率框架的“黎曼度量匹配”（Riemannian metric matching）方法。该方法利用神经网络学习carré du champ算子，通过将算子定义为数据随机扰动的条件期望，实现了样本级的训练和恒定成本的摊销推理，从而避免了传统核方法和k近邻算法对大规模高维数据计算开销大的问题。

Conclusion: 本文提出的黎曼度量匹配框架通过学习carré du champ算子，实现了高效、可扩展的几何分析，证明了在无需显式图构建的情况下，神经网络能够准确地从高维数据中捕获黎曼几何结构。

Abstract: High-dimensional datasets often concentrate near low-dimensional structures, but estimating their geometry from samples typically relies on graphs and kernels that scale poorly with dataset size and dimension. We propose Riemannian metric matching: a denoising probabilistic framework for learning the Riemannian geometry of data using neural networks. Specifically, we learn the carré du champ operator, which, using diffusion geometry, gives us access to the Riemannian geometry toolkit for downstream machine learning and statistical tasks. Our key observation is that the carré du champ operator can be formulated as a conditional expectation over random perturbations of the data, which can be exploited for sample-wise training and constant cost, amortized inference without explicit kernel construction. Empirically, metric matching rivals or improves the accuracy of $k$-NN-based diffusion geometry estimators, while enabling amortized inference that is up to $400\times$ faster, and supports graph-free geometric analysis on high-dimensional images where nearest neighbors break down.

Abstract: Tactile imaging seeks to reconstruct the internal structure of soft objects through touch sensing, with applications in medical diagnosis and robotic manipulation. Recent self-supervised learning approaches have shown promising results, but rely on global, unstructured representations and robot-controlled sensing, limiting generalization and practical use. We propose Local Encoder for Spatial Sensing (LESS), an object-centric tactile representation that exploits the local nature of touch. This compositional design enables strong generalization: models trained on single-inclusion phantoms accurately image objects with multiple inclusions and varying sizes. In addition, we enable hand-held tactile imaging via external pose tracking and human-like palpation data, and extend tactile imaging to full 3D reconstruction.

### [142] [Squeeze-Release: Iterative Pruning with Exact Structural Minimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14346)
*Roman Denkin,Ida Akerholm,Prashant Singh,Ida-Maria Sintorn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 Squeeze-Release 框架，通过将非结构化剪枝得到的稀疏网络重写为物理结构更小的稠密网络，解决了传统剪枝无法降低模型部署体积的问题，在保持精度的同时实现了显著的压缩比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非结构化剪枝虽然产生了稀疏权重，但并未改变张量形状，导致模型在实际部署时无法获得物理空间上的体积压缩。作者旨在通过数学上的精确重写，将这种“虚假”的稀疏性转化为真实的参数量缩减。

Method: 1. 最小化（Minimization）：一种精确的结构重写技术，将带有掩码（Mask）的稀疏网络转换为保持原始计算功能的更小稠密网络。
2. Squeeze-Release 循环：通过反复进行剪枝、最小化重写以及释放（Release，将重写后的权重微调作为噪声重新激活）来挖掘冗余。
3. CompensatedLayerNorm：一种保持函数不变的 LayerNorm 变体，支持在跨残差连接中实现通道层面的裁剪。

Result: 在全连接网络上实现了 39 倍的体积压缩，在 ConvNeXt-Tiny 等现代 CNN 模型上实现了 14.8 倍的压缩，且模型精度保持在可比较的水平；同时证明了该方法可扩展至 Transformer 架构。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 Squeeze-Release 框架通过“压缩-释放”的迭代循环，证明了结构化模型重写（Minimization）可以将稀疏网络转化为真实的轻量化稠密网络，并为深度学习模型的高效部署提供了新范式。

Abstract: Unstructured pruning produces sparse weight tensors, but the standard implementation keeps tensor shapes unchanged so the deployed model is no smaller than before pruning. We present an exact structural rewrite, which we call minimization, that converts a masked network into a smaller dense network with the same forward function up to floating-point rounding. The Squeeze-Release cycle iterates pruning and minimization with an intermediate release step that re-enables the exact-zero positions inside the compacted tensors as small calibrated noise, turning otherwise wasted capacity back into trainable parameters. Successive cycles use that capacity to find structural redundancy a single pass cannot reach. We additionally introduce CompensatedLayerNorm, a function-preserving replacement for LayerNorm that extends minimization to channel reduction across LayerNorm-equipped residual streams. Squeeze-Release compresses the deployable network to 39x smaller than the unpruned model on a fully-connected model network and 14.8x smaller on modern CNN (ConvNeXt-Tiny), at comparable accuracy. In addition we prove that the rewrite can be extended to transformer architectures.

</details>


### [143] [When Language Representations Interact: Separability and Cross-Lingual Effects in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14347)
*Boris Marinov,Angira Sharma,Christian Schroeder de Witt,Philip Torr,Anisoara Calinescu,Jialin Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型展现出强大的多语言能力，但其内部表征机制尚不透明。现有的因果几何可解释性框架已能解释单语言模型中概念的线性与可分性，但该框架在语言身份具有相关性和层级结构的多语言场景下是否适用，仍未得到充分探索。因此，本研究旨在探究多语言模型如何编码语言身份，以及这种表征是否存在特定的几何结构。

Method: 作者采用了因果几何分析方法（causal-geometric analysis），具体包括：1. 针对三种主流大语言模型，构建并分析了28组双语对比数据集；2. 利用协方差调整（covariance-adjusted）的因果内积技术来探测概念的线性与可分性；3. 通过几何结构分析（如单纯形结构），量化并可视化了不同语系（如日耳曼语族、罗曼语族）之间的语义依赖与层次关系。

Result: 研究发现：1. 语言概念在模型内部呈现出稳定的线性表征，在协方差调整后的空间内具有较好的可分性；2. 模型内部的偏差与语言间的相似度密切相关；3. 同语系的语言（如罗曼语族）在空间中呈现出类似于单纯形（simplex-like）的层级几何结构，表明模型内部对语言关系有明确的结构化编码。

Conclusion: 本文将因果几何可解释性框架成功扩展到了多语言模型领域。研究证实了多语言模型内部存在稳定的线性表征，且语言身份在语义空间中表现出层级化结构。这一发现不仅揭示了模型内部表征的几何特性，也为未来多语言模型的可靠性监控、干预及安全性评估提供了理论支撑，强调了处理语言间结构性依赖对于防止跨语言副作用的重要性。

Abstract: Large language models exhibit strong multilingual capabilities, however, their internal representations are difficult to interpret. Understanding these interactions is important for ensuring reliable behavior in multilingual systems. Recent work has shown that causal-geometric structure can explain how certain concepts are encoded as approximately linear and separable directions, but whether this framework extends to multilingual models, where language identity is correlated and hierarchical, is underexplored. We apply causal-geometric analysis to multilingual LLMs, studying 28 bilingual contrasts across three models, allowing us to analyze when languages behave as approximately independent factors and when structured dependencies persist. We find evidence that language concepts admit stable linear representations that are largely separable under a covariance-adjusted (causal) inner product, with structured deviations reflecting linguistic similarity. Moreover, languages within the same family (such as Germanic or Romance) exhibit a simplex-like geometric structure, suggesting hierarchical organization. These results extend causal-geometric interpretability to multilingual settings and provide insight into how separability and similarity may exist in multilingual LLM representations, motivating interpretability analyses that diagnose when and how structured dependencies between concepts can be anticipated. This has implications for trustworthy deployment, as residual structure between languages may lead to unintended cross-lingual effects when models are monitored or intervened upon.

</details>


### [144] [Can Deep Neural Networks Improve Compression of Very Large Scientific Data?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14353)
*Muhannad Alhumaidi,Guozhong Li,Spiros Skiadopoulos,Panos Kalnis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 尽管利用先进的机器学习模型（如天气预测基础模型）能显著提高科学数据的预测精度和局部压缩效果，但因其产生的残差在熵编码阶段表现不佳，整体压缩性能并未超越传统的SZ3.1压缩器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学数据的激增使得误差受限的有损压缩变得至关重要。鉴于大多数先进压缩器依赖预测-残差范式，研究人员希望探讨机器学习（ML）模型是否能作为更优的预测器，从而提升科学数据的压缩效率。

Method: 提出了一种将空间和时间深度学习模型（如Vaeformer、GraphCast和Aurora）集成到传统误差受限压缩流程（基于预测-残差范式）的框架。该框架支持自回归预测，避免了误差累积，并与SZ3.1压缩器的量化和熵编码后端进行了对比实验。

Result: 基于ERA5数据集的实验表明，ML预测器在特定变量上能提升高达91%的重构质量，并实现最高9.6倍的压缩比增长，但在数据集整体水平上，ML预测器并未能提升压缩率。

Conclusion: 该研究得出结论：机器学习预测器的预测准确度并非提升压缩效率的唯一决定因素。虽然高精度的模型可以显著提升重构质量并压缩特定变量，但残差的空间分布结构对熵编码效率具有决定性影响，从而限制了其在数据集整体压缩率上的表现。

Abstract: Error-bounded lossy compression is a fundamental technique for managing the rapidly growing volumes of scientific data produced by modern simulations and observational instruments. Most state-of-the-art-compressors follow a prediction-residual paradigm, where compression effectiveness depends on the quality of the predictor: more accurate predictions generate smaller residuals that are easier to compress. This observation raises a question: can modern machine learning models serve as superior predictors for scientific data compression? Answering this question directly is challenging because developing compression-specific ML predictors requires substantial resources. Instead, we leverage the climate domain where highly accurate pretrained weather forecasting foundation models already exist, making them an ideal testbed. We present a framework that integrates spatial and temporal deep learning models into a conventional error-bounded compression pipeline. The framework supports auto-regressive forecasting models and avoids error accumulation. Using ERA5 climate data as a representative large-scale scientific dataset, we evaluate three distinct ML predictors: a VAEformer-based codec (CRA5), a graph neural network forecaster (GraphCast), and a vision-transformer forecaster (Aurora), against the state-of-the-art compressor SZ3.1 under identical quantization and entropy-coding backends. Our evaluation over approximately 1.7 TB of data reveals a surprising result: although ML predictors generate more accurate predictions and can improve reconstruction quality by up to 91% while achieving up to 9.6x higher compression ratios for highly predictable variables, they do not improve overall dataset-level compression ratio. We show that prediction accuracy alone is insufficient: the spatial structure of the resulting residuals plays a decisive role in entropy coding efficiency.

### [145] [Flood and Harvest: The Provable Necessity of Trivia for Generating Valuable Mathematics via the Lens of Language Generation in the Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14688)
*Xiaoyu Li,Andi Han,Dai Shi,Zheng Gao,Jiaojiao Jiang,Junbin Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证明了在AI辅助证明中，即使有完美的证明检查器，也无法完全过滤掉“正确但无价值”的数学琐碎内容；事实上，为了覆盖所有有价值的数学结论，系统必须生成一定比例的琐碎内容，这是数学生成过程中的一种内在权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI辅助证明系统的发展，AI生成形式化数学的能力大幅提升。当前的主要挑战不再是证明的正确性（可由检查器保证），而是生成的数学内容是否具有“价值”。该论文旨在从理论层面探讨在证明检查器作为约束的前提下，如何高效生成具有价值的数学结论，并厘清“验证”与“价值判断”之间的本质区别。

Method: 该研究建立了一个基于嵌套语言生成的数学模型，将形式化语言（可验证集 $F$）、有价值语言（$H$）以及核心集合（$C$）进行建模。研究利用形式语言理论和博弈论视角，分析了在存在证明检查器（验证器）约束下的生成策略，通过探究生成器在处理“琐碎”陈述与“有价值”陈述时的覆盖率边界，推导出了生成质量的二分法结论。

Result: 1. 验证器无法替代“品味”，即验证器不能识别数学价值；2. 验证器能够确保结论的有效性，将错误转化为琐碎内容；3. 发现了生成效率的显著二分法：允许有限琐碎内容与允许无限琐碎内容在覆盖率上存在质的跳跃；4. 证明了生成无限多正确但无价值的琐碎内容是覆盖未知有价值数学知识的必要代价。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了形式化数学生成中的核心权衡：完美的验证器无法替代人类的“品味”。即便拥有无限的验证能力，为了覆盖未被记录的有价值数学知识，生成器必然会产生无限多（尽管渐进可忽略）的琐碎（正确但无价值）陈述。这是一个数学上的必然性，而非工程层面的失误。

Abstract: AI systems coupled to proof assistants now generate formal mathematics at scale, and the gap between what a checker can verify and what a mathematician would value has become the binding constraint. We model the generation of valuable mathematics as nested language generation in the limit: a verifiable formal language $F$, accessed through a membership oracle (the proof checker), contains an unknown valuable language $H \in \mathcal{H}$ revealed only through an adversarial enumeration of a core $C \subseteq H$ of exact density $α$ (the literature). Every output is valuable ($\in H$), trivial ($\in F \setminus H$), or a hallucination ($\notin F$). We settle four questions. First, the verifier is not taste: the collections admitting generation with breadth are exactly those of the oracle-free model, characterized fiber-wise by Angluin's condition. Second, the verifier does buy sound coverage, covering all unseen valuable statements while asserting only valid ones: possible with it, impossible without it; it relocates unavoidable errors from false to trivial. Third, and centrally, a sharp dichotomy on the tight family: generators emitting finitely many trivia achieve optimal coverage $α/2$, while any infinite trivia allowance, even at vanishing rate, jumps the optimum to $1-α/2$ (both tight, for cores presented as the candidate intersection), and one generator attains both ends. The transition is in trivia count, not rate; the gap $1-α$ is the unrecorded mass. Fourth, both regimes instantiate in a compression model of mathematics. A perfect verifier cannot substitute for taste: the unbounded stream of correct-but-worthless statements is not an engineering accident but a provable necessity, since covering unrecorded valuable mathematics requires an infinite, but asymptotically negligible, stream of certified trivia.

</details>


### [146] [MUFFLe: Efficient Model Update Compression via Generalized Deduplication for Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14354)
*Xiaobo Zhao,Daniel E. Lucani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MUFFLe是一种新型联邦学习通信压缩方案，通过引入广义去重技术，在保证模型精度的前提下，显著降低了客户端模型更新上传的通信成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习在边缘环境中受限于模型更新上传的通信成本，亟需高效的压缩方案来缓解上行带宽瓶颈。

Method: 提出了MUFFLe框架，将广义去重（GD）机制集成到FedAvg联邦学习流程中。该方法通过对模型更新向量中的重复模式进行去重，实现了一种固定速率、可变计数的压缩方案。

Result: 在IID MNIST数据集和20个客户端的实验中，MUFFLe达到92.93%的目标准确率仅需38MB的累计上传流量，明显优于8-bit量化（75MB）、Top-k稀疏化（86MB）以及未压缩的FedAvg（310MB）。

Conclusion: 将广义去重（GD）技术应用于联邦学习的更新压缩是可行的，能够显著降低通信开销，同时保持模型准确率。

Abstract: Federated learning is well suited to edge environments but is often limited by the uplink cost of transmitting model updates. This Work-in-Progress paper presents MUFFLe, a communication-efficient update compression scheme that integrates generalized deduplication (GD) into the FedAvg pipeline. MUFFLe deduplicates repeated patterns across the update vector, yielding a fixed-rate, variable-count compression scheme. Preliminary experiments on IID MNIST with 20 clients show that MUFFLe reaches the target accuracy of $92.93\%$ with 38~MB cumulative uplink communication, compared with 75~MB for 8-bit quantization, 86~MB for Top-$k$ sparsification, and 310~MB for uncompressed FedAvg. These results demonstrate the feasibility of applying GD to communication-efficient federated learning.

### [147] [Persona-Pruner: Sculpting Lightweight Models for Role-Playing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14695)
*Jinsu Kim,Jihoon Tack,Noah Lee,Jongheon Jeong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对角色扮演大模型计算成本过高的问题，本文提出了 Persona-Pruner 框架，通过从通用模型中提取特定角色的子网络，在大幅降低参数量的同时，保持了极佳的角色扮演质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型（LM）在角色扮演任务中表现出色，但为每个角色分配一个完整的通用模型在实际应用中（如多 NPC 交互场景）计算成本过高。现有的剪枝技术无法在去除冗余参数的同时保持角色扮演的连贯性和准确性，因此作者希望通过探索“特定角色仅依赖模型部分能力”的假设，开发出一种轻量级的角色扮演框架。

Method: 本文提出了 Persona-Pruner 框架。该方法的核心在于从一个通用大模型中识别并分离出特定于某个角色的子网络（sub-networks），而不是简单地剪枝不重要的权重。通过这种方式，它能够区分角色所需的本质特征与通用知识，从而在极度压缩模型规模的同时保留关键的角色扮演能力。

Result: 在 RoleBench 基准测试中，Persona-Pruner 表现优于现有的剪枝技术，在 LLM-as-a-judge 评分上，相比最强的基准方法，性能下降幅度减少了高达 93.8%，同时依然维持了模型的通用能力。

Conclusion: Persona-Pruner 证明了无需保留完整的通用语言模型即可实现高效且高质量的角色扮演。通过识别并提取特定于角色的子网络，该框架成功在大幅降低计算成本的同时，保持了与原模型相当的角色扮演能力和通用任务能力，为轻量化、多角色的 AI 应用提供了新思路。

Abstract: Language Models (LMs) have shown remarkable potential as role-playing chatbots, delivering consistent, stylized interactions when given a specification of a character or user persona. However, applying these capabilities to real-world applications (e.g., ecosystems with numerous NPCs interacting simultaneously) exposes a critical inefficiency due to the excessive computational cost. In this paper, we question the necessity of dedicating a full, generalist model to a single persona, hypothesizing that a specific character identity relies on only a fraction of the model's total capacity. We observe that naively pruning LMs often severely degrades the role-playing performance for a specific persona; it does not distinguish between redundant knowledge and essential character traits. We propose Persona-Pruner, a framework that sculpts a lightweight role-playing model by isolating persona-specific sub-networks from a single description. Our experiments consistently show that Persona-Pruner preserves role-playing performance substantially more effectively than existing state-of-the-art LLM pruning techniques, reducing the performance drop from the dense model by up to 93.8% over the strongest baseline on RoleBench in LLM-as-a-judge score, while still maintaining general LLM capabilities. Code is available at https://github.com/jsu-kim/Persona-Pruner.

</details>

TL;DR: SemPipes是一种新型编程模型，它将大模型转化为可控、可优化的声明式算子，嵌入机器学习流水线中，旨在解决传统LLM辅助开发中集成难、优化难的问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: SemPipes实现了在数据科学流水线中可控、可优化地集成LLM能力，通过SemPiper界面展示了其在代码生成、计算图优化及端到端应用中的实用性。

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) pipelines require extensive data preparation, feature engineering, and integration across heterogeneous sources, making them tedious and error-prone to develop. While large language models (LLMs) have recently shown promise for assisting programming tasks, chat-based interfaces provide limited control over pipeline behavior and often produce code that is difficult to optimize or integrate into production systems. We demonstrate SemPipes, a novel programming model that extends ML pipelines with declarative, LLM-powered semantic data operators. SemPipes allows developers to specify high-level natural language instructions for data-centric operations, while seamlessly combining these operators with arbitrary Python code from standard data science libraries. For the semantic operators, it synthesizes specialized implementations at pipeline training time, conditioned on dataset characteristics and pipeline context, enabling the flexible yet controlled integration of LLM capabilities. We demonstrate SemPipes through SemPiper, an interactive interface that visualizes computational graphs of the pipelines, synthesized operator implementations, and optimization trajectories produced by an evolutionary search procedure. Attendees can explore three end-to-end scenarios, modify pipelines, inspect generated code, and observe how semantic operators are synthesized and iteratively optimized. The demonstration highlights how declarative semantic operators enable controllable, optimizable, and practical integration of LLMs into ML pipeline development.

### [149] [Discovery under Hypothesis Redundancy: A Geometric Theory of Discovery Bottlenecks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14386)
*Li Xia,Baoxun Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出“搜索压缩假设”，指出大模型辅助的科学发现只有在满足光谱压缩、正交逃逸和残差信号对齐这三个特定几何条件时才有效，从而解释了为何单纯追求新颖性往往无法带来实质性突破。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学发现存在饱和现象，即使假设空间很大，如果新假设不能提供独立信息，发现进程也会停滞。研究者试图揭示大模型在科学发现中“何时”以及“为何”能起到辅助作用，并解决如何从单纯追求新颖性转向高效、有针对性的探索问题。

Method: 研究者提出了混合发现系统，结合了结构化局部搜索和基于大模型（LLM）的非局部提案。通过形式化定义光谱压缩、正交逃逸和残差信号对齐三个几何条件，并在合成环境、A股因子发现及符号回归基准测试中进行验证，通过信号植入和对照实验评估了这些条件的必要性。

Result: 实验结果表明，仅仅依靠新颖性（随机正交跳转）不足以提高收益；只有当满足几何对齐条件时，混合发现系统才能带来显著增益。在弱表示但包含目标的维度上，混合搜索表现出明显优势，且随着假设空间趋于满秩，这种增益会逐渐消失。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了“搜索压缩假设”，即大模型辅助的非局部探索并非总是有效。其优势仅在满足光谱压缩、正交逃逸和残差信号对齐这三个几何条件时才会显现。该框架将大模型引导的发现从盲目的新颖性搜索转变为一种诊断程序，用以判断何时进行定向探索是有益的。

Abstract: Scientific discovery saturates when new hypotheses cease to provide independent information, even if the nominal hypothesis space remains large. We study hybrid discovery systems that combine structured local search with LLM-generated non-local proposals and pose the Search Compression Hypothesis: non-local exploration helps only when three geometric conditions co-occur: spectral compression, orthogonal escape from the explored span, and residual signal alignment with the target. We formalize these conditions, derive necessary conditions for hybrid advantage, and test the mechanism in controlled synthetic environments, large-scale A-share factor discovery, and symbolic-regression benchmarks; a public tabular operational sanity check tests the associated budget-allocation implication. Signal-planting and directed-versus-random experiments show that novelty alone is insufficient: random orthogonal jumps expand coverage but do not improve yield without predictive alignment. Across compression sweeps, real factor archives, and LLM-SRBench tasks, hybrid gains concentrate in weakly represented but target-bearing directions and vanish as the hypothesis space approaches full rank. The framework turns LLM-guided discovery from generic novelty search into a diagnostic procedure for deciding when directed non-local exploration is warranted.

### [150] [A Low-Rank Subspace Analysis of LLM Interventions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14388)
*Angira Sharma,Christian Schroeder de Witt,Philip Torr,Anisoara Calinescu,Jialin Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过将LLM行为建模为激活空间中的子空间，分析了行为间的相互干扰。研究表明，由于行为表征的重叠和非对称交互，对单一行为的干预往往会引起其他行为的意外改变，这为实现精确的LLM行为控制带来了核心挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前针对LLM特定行为（如拒绝或奉承）的干预措施往往会产生难以预料的副作用，导致缺乏针对性的精确控制，难以实现可靠的安全保障。因此，有必要深入理解这些行为背后的相互作用机制，以实现更精准的模型调控。

Method: 本文提出了一种用于分析LLM行为交互的诊断框架，主要包括：1. 将模型激活空间中的特定行为建模为低秩子空间；2. 通过量化行为子空间之间的重叠程度（平均平方余弦主角）以及行为子空间与模型决策子空间之间的角度，来分析干预措施如何跨行为传播。研究在7B至70B参数规模的多种指令微调模型上，针对拒绝、越狱和奉承等行为进行了实验验证。

Result: 实验发现：1. 不同的模型行为共享内部表征，对一种行为的干预会以非对称方式影响其他行为；2. 某些行为充当了“上游控制点”，其干预影响会广泛传播；3. 行为子空间重叠度越高、源行为子空间越接近决策子空间，干预产生的跨行为影响就越大。

Conclusion: 本文的研究结果揭示了大型语言模型（LLM）行为控制的固有挑战：由于不同行为之间存在共享的表征空间和非对称的交互作用，试图独立修改某项特定行为往往会引发意外的副作用。这意味着在设计安全性控制时，必须考虑到行为间潜在的耦合关系，而非简单地进行孤立干预。

Abstract: Interventions designed to modify a particular behavior in LLMs, such as refusal or sycophancy, often produce unintended changes in other behaviors. This lack of targeted control makes it difficult to design and implement reliable safety controls. To understand these side-effects, we introduce a diagnostic framework for analyzing interacting behaviors in LLMs. We model behaviors as low-rank subspaces in activation space, and study how interventions influence across behaviors. Across multiple instruction-tuned models (7B-70B) and across refusal, jailbreak, and sycophancy settings, we find that different behaviors share internal representations, and intervening on one behavior alters others in asymmetric ways. Some behaviors act as upstream control points whose interventions propagate broadly across other behaviors, while others remain more isolated. We relate these effects to two geometric quantities: (i) the overlap between behavior subspaces, measured as the average squared cosine of principal angles, and (ii) the angle between each behavior subspace and the decision subspace (capturing the model's final decision e.g., refuse vs. comply). Empirically, intervention effects on other behaviors tend to be larger for behavior pairs with higher subspace overlap, and for source behaviors whose subspaces lie closer (smaller angle) to the decision subspace. These findings highlight a challenge for targeted behavior control: behaviors are difficult to modify independently, as interventions can propagate through shared representations and asymmetric interactions.

</details>


### [151] [Running the Gauntlet: Re-evaluating the Capabilities of Agents Beyond Familiar Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14397)
*Mykola Vysotskyi,Runqi Lin,Grzegorz Biziel,Michal Zakrzewski,Sebastian Montagna,Damian Rynczak,Shreyansh Padarha,Kumail Alhamoud,Zihao Fu,William Lugoloobi,Kai Rawal,Hanna Yershova,Xander Davies,Taras Rumezhak,Guohao Li,Fazl Barez,Baoyuan Wu,Arkadiusz Drohomirecki,Yarin Gal,Chris Russell,Christopher Summerfield,Adam Mahdi,Volodymyr Karpiv,Philip Torr,Adel Bibi*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为 GauntletBench 的新型基准测试，旨在评估智能体在时间感知、图形理解和 3D 推理等复杂视觉维度下的泛化能力，研究发现当前顶尖智能体在专业应用场景中表现远逊于人类，存在显著的能力鸿沟。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了 GauntletBench，这是一个基于 Web 的智能体评测基准，包含：1. 涵盖五个专业领域（视频编辑、工作流构建、3D 建模、飞行分析、电路设计）的 100 项视觉密集型任务；2. 一个模块化的流水线，包括兼容各类智能体框架的环境、受控的 Web 应用程序、结构化任务套件；3. 一套多维度的自动化评估引擎。

Result: 实验结果表明，即便是目前最先进的智能体在 GauntletBench 上的成功率仅为 19.1%，而普通人类用户在相同任务下的成功率超过 80%，证明当前智能体与复杂真实应用需求之间存在显著差距。

Conclusion: 现有的前沿智能体系统在复杂、专业且需要多维感知与推理的真实场景中表现依然较差，远未达到人类水平。GauntletBench 揭示了现有智能体在时间感知、图形理解和三维推理等关键维度上的局限性，为未来开发更具通用性和鲁棒性的智能体提供了明确的改进方向。

Abstract: As agentic systems continue to evolve and are widely deployed in real-world scenarios, there is a growing demand to faithfully evaluate their capabilities. However, current benchmarks are typically built on popular applications with relatively simple tasks and focus on a narrow set of capabilities while overlooking broader dimensions, resulting in saturated performance on modern agents and failing to probe their limitations. To this end, we introduce GauntletBench, a web-based benchmark for evaluating agent generalisation in challenging scenarios, focusing on three underexplored capabilities (temporal perception, graphical understanding, and 3D reasoning), across five less-covered professional applications (Video Editor, Workflow Builder, 3D Modeller, Flight Analyser, and Circuit Designer), each with 20 vision-intensive tasks (100 in total). Our benchmark provides a modular pipeline that comprises an environment compatible with both open- and closed-source agent frameworks, a controlled web-based application, a well-structured task suite, and an automated evaluation engine with diverse metrics. Contrary to widespread expectations, our empirical results reveal that frontier agentic systems remain far from achieving human-level performance. Even the state-of-the-art agent achieves only a 19.1% success rate on our GauntletBench, highlighting the limitations in these overlooked capabilities and generalisation. By comparison, non-expert human annotators achieve over 80% success on our challenging yet feasible tasks, revealing the substantial gap between current agent capabilities and those required for complex real-world scenarios.

### [152] [A theoretical model for task routing in mixture-of-expert transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14398)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本研究从理论上证实了单层MoE Transformer能够通过任务专有专家实现知识编码，且专家规模仅取决于任务的内在复杂度，为理解大型语言模型中观测到的“局部化知识电路”现象提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Mixture-of-experts (MoE) layers enable the scaling of transformer models while keeping the inference compute fixed. While task-expert specialization has been observed in empirical studies of frontier MoE transformer models, existing theoretical work analyzes this using continuous mixture models that cannot be used to model natural language effectively. An important open question is to \textit{theoretically explain task-expert specialization in transformer MoE models using discrete models of language}. To address this, we represent structured knowledge via syntactic templates and finite key-value dictionaries, and prove formally that a single-layer MoE transformer can encode knowledge by using experts that specialize in the corresponding tasks. Our construction shows how queries are routed to unique, task-specific experts whose size depends solely on the intrinsic complexity of the given task (i.e. the combined size of its syntactic templates and factual dictionary). Our construction provides a theoretical support for empirical results on localized knowledge circuits in MoE models. ### [153] [Federated Learning for Feature Generalization with Convex Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14416)
*Dongwon Kim,Donghee Kim,Sung Kuk Shyn,Kwangsu Kim*

TL;DR: FedCONST 是一种新型联邦学习框架，通过自适应调节参数更新和引入线性凸约束，缓解了数据异构带来的过拟合与特征扭曲问题，实现了更强的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 FedCONST 算法，通过基于全局模型参数强度自适应调节更新幅度，防止对已充分学习参数的过度强化；利用线性凸约束在聚合过程中保持训练稳定性并保留本地特征的泛化能力；并结合梯度信噪比（GSNR）分析验证了其在提升特征可迁移性方面的作用。

Result: 实验表明，FedCONST 能有效对齐本地与全局目标，显著减轻过拟合，并在多种联邦学习环境下展现出优于现有主流方法（State-of-the-art）的泛化性能。

Conclusion: FedCONST 通过引入自适应更新调节和线性凸约束，有效平衡了联邦学习中全局模型与本地数据的差异，解决了模型过拟合和特征扭曲问题，是提升联邦学习泛化能力的一种有效且稳健的方案。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) often struggles with generalization due to heterogeneous client data. Local models are prone to overfitting their local data distributions, and even transferable features can be distorted during aggregation. To address these challenges, we propose FedCONST, an approach that adaptively modulates update magnitudes based on the parameter strength of the global model. This prevents over-emphasizing well-learned parameters while reinforcing underdeveloped ones. Specifically, FedCONST employs linear convex constraints to ensure training stability and preserve locally learned generalization capabilities during aggregation. A Gradient Signal to Noise Ratio (GSNR) analysis further validates the effectiveness of FedCONST in enhancing feature transferability and robustness. As a result, FedCONST effectively aligns local and global objectives, mitigating overfitting and promoting stronger generalization across diverse FL environments, achieving state-of-the-art performance.

### [154] [EM-NeSy: Expectation Maximization for Neurosymbolic Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14463)
*Annegret Seibt,Luc De Raedt,Giuseppe Marra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于 EM 算法的神经符号学习框架 EM-NeSy，通过将学习过程解耦为期望步（推理）和最大化步（参数更新），成功去除了对符号组件可微性的依赖，显著提升了模型的灵活性与扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经符号（NeSy）模型通常要求符号组件必须可微，这限制了模型在复杂符号逻辑处理及近似推理中的应用。为了解决这一局限，研究者寻求一种无需强制要求符号组件可微的通用训练框架。

Method: 提出 EM-NeSy 框架，将神经符号学习建模为期望最大化（EM）过程：E 步通过概率推理计算神经网络预测符号的后验分布，M 步则仅利用梯度下降更新神经网络参数，无需符号组件具备可微性。

Result: 实验结果表明，EM-NeSy 框架不仅具备良好的可扩展性和计算效率，在精确推理条件下还能等效于标准的端到端梯度学习设置，且在处理需要近似推理的任务时表现优越。

Conclusion: EM-NeSy 成功将 EM 算法引入神经符号学习中，为处理不可微符号逻辑及复杂近似推理提供了一个通用且高效的框架，证明了该方法在保持学习效果的同时，具有更好的可扩展性。

Abstract: Neurosymbolic (NeSy) models integrate neural networks and symbolic reasoning for robust and interpretable AI. State-of-the-art NeSy models require that the symbolic component is expressed in a differentiable way, often complicating the use of approximate inference. We propose EM-NeSy which casts probabilistic NeSy learning as an instance of the Expectation-Maximization (EM) algorithm. In the expectation step, we compute the posterior over the neurally predicted symbols conditioned on the label via probabilistic inference. In the maximization step, we update the neural parameters based on this posterior using gradient descent only through the neural component. This formulation unlocks the full potential of the EM algorithm for NeSy learning. It allows NeSy to extend naturally to approximate reasoning without any additional modifications or differentiability requirements of the symbolic component. Furthermore, it recovers the standard end-to-end gradient-based NeSy setting under exact inference. Our experimental results demonstrate the scalability and computational efficiency of EM-NeSy.

### [155] [Recipe-Controlled Decoder Audit for Structural Knowledge-Graph Completion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14492)
*Xihang Shan,Ye Luo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过“配方可控解码器审计（RCDA）”揭示了知识图谱补全任务中，解码器的选择对实验结果的影响往往被低估；研究建议在宣称编码器贡献前，应首先控制并审计解码器与训练配方的交互作用，以确保评估的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在知识图谱补全（KGC）研究中，性能提升往往被归功于编码器的设计，但解码器的选择对实验结果的影响常被忽视或混淆。作者旨在澄清“编码器改进”与“解码器效应”之间的贡献差异，以提高实验评估的严谨性和可复现性。

Method: 提出了“配方可控解码器审计（RCDA）”方法。通过在统一的训练配方（recipe）下，系统地交换不同的解码器（如ComplEx与DistMult，并辅以RotatE/TransE），在七个知识图谱基准上进行对照实验，并深入分析了小规模知识图谱中解码器选择对实验结果稳定性及复现性的影响。

Result: 在标准知识图谱上，ComplEx和DistMult之间的性能差异较小但一致；在小规模知识图谱上，解码器效应变得显著且具有高度的配方敏感性。实验还发现解码器的选择与编码器深度存在交互作用，且简单的ComplEx模型在特定参数配置下即能达到极具竞争力的性能。

Conclusion: 研究提出了一个紧凑的审计协议：要求研究者在报告模型性能时，必须提供匹配的解码器对比行、记录小型知识图谱的来源，并在声称编码器改进之前进行解码器与深度（decoder x depth）的交叉验证。结论表明，解码器的选择在不同数据集和训练配置下存在不确定性，不应将其视为固定的“最优解”。

Abstract: We present a recipe-controlled decoder audit (RCDA) for structural transductive knowledge-graph completion (KGC). The audit asks a simple reporting question: before attributing gains to an encoder or training recipe, what changes when the decoder is swapped under the same recipe? Using ComplEx and DistMult as the primary controlled pair, with targeted RotatE/TransE spot-checks, we evaluate seven benchmarks. On five standard KGs, ComplEx-vs-DistMult differences are modest but consistent under our recipe (+0.005 to +0.012 MRR), whereas CompGCN-style encoder effects vary more by dataset. On small KGs, decoder effects become the main diagnostic: Kinship shows a stable ComplEx advantage of +0.143 MRR (6 seeds), while UMLS favours ComplEx by +0.022 MRR in a clean 6-seed server rerun but reverses in an earlier provenance variant. We therefore treat small-KG decoder choice as recipe- and provenance-sensitive rather than as a fixed dataset winner. We further show that decoder choice interacts with encoder depth on WN18RR, and that under our recipe L=0 ComplEx on YAGO3-10 reaches 0.6971 +/- 0.0048 MRR at d=128. The result is a compact audit protocol: report matched decoder rows, log small-KG provenance, and sweep decoder x depth before making encoder-level claims.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: PepALD 采用了自回归潜在扩散（ALD）模型：1. 使用结构化化学嵌入表示 HELM 单体；2. 在化学信息丰富的潜在空间中通过上下文条件扩散生成残基；3. 在生成过程中预测基于 R 基团的成环闭合；4. 利用赢家保护的扩散适配偏好优化（DAPO）将去噪器与结合亲和力奖励对齐。

Result: 计算机模拟实验表明，PepALD 在生成质量以及针对特定亲和力奖励的优化性能方面，均优于现有的代表性肽生成基线模型。

Conclusion: PepALD 成功建立了一种结合潜在空间扩散与自回归生成的框架，为宏环肽的从头设计提供了一种高效、且具备化学可控性的新范式，能够有效平衡药物性质与结合亲和力。

Abstract: Macrocyclic peptides are promising therapeutic candidates for intracellular targets, but their design requires simultaneous control over non-natural monomer chemistry, ring topology, membrane permeability, and target binding. Existing SMILES- or HELM-string generative models either operate in long atom-level sequence spaces or treat monomers as symbolic tokens with limited chemical grounding. We introduce PepALD, an Autoregressive Latent Diffusion (ALD) foundation model for \textit{de novo} macrocyclic peptide generation. The model represents HELM monomers with structured chemical embeddings, generates each residue through context-conditioned diffusion in chemically informed latent space, predicts R-group-aware ring closures during autoregressive generation, and aligns the denoiser to affinity rewards using winner-protected diffusion-adapted preference optimization. In silico experiments demonstrate PepALD's generation quality and reward-optimization performance against representative peptide generation baselines.
